### [1] [EDEN: A Large-Scale Corpus of Clinical Notes for Italian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12569)
*Tiziano Labruna,Guido Bertolini,Pietro Ferrazzi,Bernardo Magnini*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文介绍了EDEN数据集，这是目前最大的开源意大利语急诊临床笔记语料库（约400万份），涵盖人工标注的急诊病例信息，并提出了用于测试大语言模型医疗信息提取能力的CRF-filling基准任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了解决医疗领域特别是意大利语临床文本数据稀缺的问题，弥补现有大规模语料库在临床应用支持上的不足，并为评估大语言模型在急诊医学场景下的结构化信息提取能力提供基准。

Method: 研究者构建了一个包含约400万份匿名化意大利急诊临床笔记的语料库，并对其中6000份笔记进行了专家人工标注（涉及呼吸困难和意识丧失两种情况，包含132个临床指标）。此外，作者提出了CRF-filling（病例报告表填充）基准任务，并使用Gemma-27B和MedGemma-27B模型进行了零样本基准测试。

Result: 成功构建了名为EDEN的大规模、经匿名处理的意大利急诊临床笔记数据集；定义了CRF-filling基准任务；并提供了当前主流大模型在处理该任务时的初步性能基准。

Conclusion: EDEN是目前意大利语临床笔记领域最大的公开语料库，为医疗领域的大语言模型研究提供了重要的基准和资源，特别是在结构化信息提取（CRF-filling）任务上具有显著的研究价值。

Abstract: We present EDEN (Emergency Department Electronic Notes), a new and unique large-scale corpus of clinical notes produced in Emergency Departments of Italian hospitals. The corpus, in its current version, is composed of approximately 4 million clinical notes fully anonymized, covering diverse phases of patient care during the stay in the emergency department. In addition, a subset of about six thousand notes has been manually annotated by clinical experts through a structured Case Report Form (CRF) containing 132 items relevant for two patient situations in emergency departments, dyspnea and loss of consciousness. Items may assume numerical values (e.g., for blood saturation), categorical (e.g., for level of consciousness ), binary (e.g., for presence of traumas), and mixed value types. The annotation process involved multiple clinicians and underwent iterative revision to resolve ambiguities in item formulation, resulting in a richly structured (although high imbalanced) resource. The dataset aims to fill a relevant gap of data able to support both the development and the use of Large Language Models in concrete medical applications. We describe the data collection protocol, the on-site anonymisation pipeline, corpus statistics, and the annotation scheme. Finally, we propose CRF-filling as a novel structured information extraction benchmark, and provide zero-shot baseline resulting from Gemma-27B and MedGemma-27B. To the best of our knowledge, the EDEN dataset is the largest freely available corpus of clinical notes existing for the Italian language.

</details>


### [2] [Helping Figures Tell their Story! Paper-Grounded Video Generation Explaining Complex Scientific Figures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12576)
*Ishani Mondal,Javad Baghirov,Jordan Boyd-Graber*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 MINARD 模型，旨在将复杂的科学图表转化为带有论文原文依据的分步讲解视频，并发布了 FigTalk 基准测试以评估图表与叙事的对齐效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的视频生成系统和基准测试缺乏将科学图表转化为带叙事功能的教学视频的能力。研究人员难以通过单一图表快速理解复杂的研究流程，因此需要一种能结合论文原文、按步骤对图表进行可视化讲解的自动化方案。

Method: 作者提出了名为 MINARD（通过区域分解的多模态叙事架构解释）的流水线。该方法包含以下步骤：1. 对科学图表进行区域分解（region decomposition）；2. 根据论文上下文生成分步叙事（paper-grounded narration）；3. 将生成的叙事序列与图表中的特定视觉区域进行对齐和定位。此外，作者还发布了 FigTalk 基准测试，用于评估叙事与图表组件的顺序及空间关联准确性。

Result: 在 FigTalk 基准测试中，MINARD 生成的叙事展现了类人的表达能力且高度忠实于原始论文。在叙事驱动的图表空间定位任务中，MINARD 在自动评估指标和人工评估中均显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: MINARD 框架通过将科学图表拆解为可理解的组件，实现了高质量的叙事生成与区域定位。该研究证明了利用论文上下文增强视觉理解的可行性，并为科学图表的自动化讲解提供了新的范式和评估标准。

Abstract: Scientific figures compress complex pipelines into a single canvas, yet understanding them requires paper-grounded, step-by-step narration aligned with visual highlights a capability missing from current video generation systems and benchmarks. To address this, we introduce paper-grounded figure-to-video generation: generating narrated, region-grounded walkthrough videos from a figure and its paper. We propose MINARD (Multimodal Interpretation of Narrated Architecture via Region Decomposition), a pipeline that generates paper-grounded narrations and sequentially grounds them to figure regions. We also release FigTalk, a benchmark with new sequential and component-level grounding metrics derived. On FigTalk, MINARD generates humanlike, paper-faithful narrations and outperforms narration-conditioned figure spatial grounding compared to existing approaches in both automatic and human evaluation

</details>


### [3] [MARD: Mirror-Augmented Reasoning Distillation for Mechanism-Level Drug-Drug Interaction Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12578)
*Mohammadreza Riyazat,Vian Lelo,Rameen Jafri,Yumna Khan,Abeer Badawi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为MARD-7B的机制级药物相互作用（DDI）预测框架，通过结合结构化知识检索与过程奖励模型，实现了比现有大模型更高效、更具泛化能力的药理推理，成功解决了模型对药物频率的盲目记忆问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的DDI预测往往局限于简单的“是/否”分类，缺乏对相互作用机制（如涉及的酶、药效轴及方向）的深入解释。为了解决这一痛点，需要一种能够提供可审计、机制级推理的预测方案。

Method: 提出了一种包含7大类147个子类的机制级DDI分类体系，并引入了MARD（镜像增强推理蒸馏）框架。核心创新包括：1. 针对方向标签的单令牌KL散度损失；2. 结合程序化硬负样本的每步奖励模型加权DPO（直接偏好优化）；3. 防数据泄露的机制感知检索通道。该流程利用DrugBank结构化字段进行自动验证，无需人类反馈。

Result: 在2026年4月的DrugBank数据集测试中，MARD-7B在处理新药对时表现出优异的泛化能力，准确率较最佳基线提升13.9个百分点，较GPT-4o提升6.7个百分点，且推理成本仅为前沿API的1%。研究还证实模型表现出“反记忆化”特征，在罕见药物上的准确率反而更高，证明其确实掌握了药理学推理能力。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了通过结合过程奖励模型（PRM）和结构化知识检索，能够显著提升大语言模型在药物相互作用（DDI）领域的泛化能力与推理精度，为医疗AI提供了一种高效且可审计的解决方案。

Abstract: Mechanism-level drug-drug interaction (DDI) prediction requires identifying which enzyme or pharmacodynamic axis is implicated, in which direction, and with which evidence -- not merely whether two drugs interact. We introduce a reproducible mechanism-level DDI labelling and evaluation protocol with a structured 7-family/147-subtype taxonomy, leakage-safe cold-split protocols, and auditable reasoning metrics for evaluating pharmacological prediction beyond flat interaction classification. We propose a pipeline that produces a 7B reasoning MARD (Mirror-Augmented Reasoning Distillation), combining three training innovations: a single-token KL divergence on direction tag that ties the model's prediction, per-loss PRM-weighted DPO with programmatic hard negatives, and a leakage-safe mechanism-aware retrieval channel. Process-reward step labels are automatically verifiable against DrugBank-structured fields, requiring no human or LLM judges. On the April-2026 DrugBank release, our MARD-7B is the only system in a 32-system comparison whose accuracy survives drug-pair novelty, beating the best baseline by +13.9 pp and GPT-4o by +6.7 pp at ~1% of frontier API cost. Further analysis reveals an anti-memorisation signature where accuracy improves on rarely seen drugs, suggesting that gain comes from structured pharmacological reasoning rather than drug-frequency memorisation. We release corpus, DDI-PRM, retrieval index, and training code.

</details>


### [4] [Constrained Semantic Decompression in LLMs through Persian Proverb-Conditioned Story Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12599)
*Zahra Habibzadeh,Paria Khoshtab,Amir Mesbah,Yadollah Yaghoobzadeh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了LLM将抽象谚语转化为叙事的问题，发现模型存在“解压缩差距”，即难以忠实呈现谚语的深层道德与因果结构，但通过显式推理和迭代优化可以有效缓解该问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在研究大语言模型如何将抽象的文化知识（如谚语）转化为连贯、具有道德内涵且忠实于原意的叙事，即解决“从抽象到实现”的语义解压缩挑战。

Method: 1. 构建了波斯语谚语对齐叙事数据集（PAND），包含谚语、人工编写的故事及明确含义；2. 提出了“受限语义解压缩”任务框架；3. 采用混合评估体系，结合人类校准的“LLM-as-a-Judge”评估方法与结构化指标；4. 测试了多种提示（Prompting）策略及迭代优化方法。

Result: 研究发现大语言模型存在“解压缩差距”，即模型虽然能生成表面流畅的文本，但往往无法精准地实例化谚语中隐含的道德与因果结构。此外，通过显式推理和迭代优化，模型表现有所提升，表明问题的根源在于将抽象含义转化为叙事形式的困难，而非缺乏相关知识。

Conclusion: 尽管大语言模型在生成流畅文本方面表现优异，但在将高度抽象的文化知识（如谚语）解压缩为具有一致逻辑和道德内涵的叙事时仍存在显著缺陷。显式的推理和迭代优化策略能有效缩小这一“解压缩差距”。

Abstract: Transforming a dense, abstract proverb into an engaging and morally faithful narrative requires deep cultural understanding and robust semantic grounding. We frame this problem as a \emph{constrained semantic decompression} task and study proverb-conditioned story generation as a testbed for abstraction-to-realization in large language models (LLMs). Focusing on Persian, we introduce the Proverb Aligned Narrative Dataset (PAND), pairing proverbs with human-written stories and explicit meanings. By a hybrid evaluation framework that combines human-calibrated LLM-as-a-Judge with structural metrics, we analyze model behavior across multiple prompting regimes. Our findings reveal a persistent \emph{decompression gap}: current LLMs often achieve strong surface-level fluency while failing to faithfully instantiate the underlying moral and causal structure encoded in proverbs. We further show that explicit reasoning and iterative refinement can partially mitigate these failures, suggesting that many decompression errors arise from difficulties in translating abstract meaning into narrative form rather than a complete lack of relevant knowledge. Our proposed task naturally extends to other forms of compressed cultural knowledge.

</details>


### [5] [Shopping Reasoning Bench: An Expert-Authored Benchmark for Multi-Turn Conversational Shopping Assistants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12608)
*Shuxian Fan,Seonwoo Min,Youna Hu,Botao Xia,Jayakrishnan Unnikrishnan,Rowan Musselmann,Yifan Gao,Qingyu Yin,Priyanka Nigam,Bing Yin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了Shopping Reasoning Bench，这是一个专门评估对话式购物助手推理能力的专家级基准测试。研究显示，当前顶级大模型在处理复杂购物需求（如多轮权衡和深度偏好分析）时仍存在显著的性能瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基准测试无法全面评估对话式购物助手所需的开放式多轮推理、领域专业知识以及标准级的质量要求。购物推理具有独特的需求，需要平衡主观偏好、预算限制和跨产品权衡，而之前的电子商务和通用基准测试缺乏这些能力的度量标准。

Method: 提出了“购物推理基准测试”（Shopping Reasoning Bench），包含由零售领域专家编写的525项购物任务（232项单轮，293项多轮），并配有10863个权重化的二进制评估准则。该基准将任务分为5大类和15个子类，用于评估模型在偏好提炼、权衡分析和兼容性评估等方面的能力。研究者利用该基准测试了GPT、Claude和Gemini三个系列的九款模型。

Result: 研究发现，九款模型的整体通过率仅为57%至77%。在多轮对话任务中，所有模型在“超额/进阶”标准上的得分比“必要”标准低13至29分，且随着对话的深入，模型表现普遍下降了4至18分。

Conclusion: 目前的模型能够处理基础的购物辅助任务，但在进行专家级的复杂购物决策建议时表现不佳，特别是在多轮对话的持续性推理和“超额”需求满足方面存在明显不足。该基准测试为未来购物助手的发展提供了一个具有挑战性的评估平台。

Abstract: Conversational shopping assistants now serve hundreds of millions of customers, yet no existing benchmark jointly evaluates the open-ended multi-turn reasoning, domain expertise, and criterion-level quality that real shopping conversations demand. Shopping reasoning is unique among language model applications. Unlike factual question answering or verifiable code generation, it requires balancing subjective preferences, budget constraints, and cross-product trade-offs across multi-turn dialogue, capabilities absent from previous e-commerce and general-purpose benchmarks. We introduce the Shopping Reasoning Bench, an expert-authored benchmark of 525 missions (232 single-turn, 293 multi-turn) with 10863 importance-weighted binary rubrics authored by retail domain experts. These criteria are organized under a taxonomy of five reasoning categories and fifteen subcategories covering diverse demands such as preference refinement, trade-off analysis, and compatibility assessment. An evaluation of nine models across three families (GPT, Claude, Gemini) shows that pass rates reach only 57--77% overall. On multi-turn missions, all models score 13--29 points lower on optional above-and-beyond criteria than on required ones, and performance degrades 4--18 points as conversations progress. These gaps show that current models handle basic shopping assistance but fall short of expert-level advice, making Shopping Reasoning Bench a challenging testbed for future shopping assistant development.

</details>


### [6] [How Fine-Grained Should a RAG Benchmark Be? A Hierarchical Framework for Synthetic Question Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12789)
*Chase M. Fensore,Kaustubh Dhole,Jason Fan,Eugene Agichtein,Joyce C. Ho*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了 HieraRAG 框架，通过引入最优颗粒度和相干比指标，帮助研究者系统性地确定 RAG 系统评估中的最佳维度划分颗粒度，以实现更具区分度的性能评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前 RAG 系统评估缺乏关于评估基准应涵盖哪些维度以及在何种颗粒度下进行评估的经验指导，导致评估系统难以精准衡量不同特征问题的表现。

Method: 提出了 HieraRAG 层次化框架，通过定义“最优颗粒度”为使生成质量在类别间区分度（标准差）最大化的水平，并引入“相干比（Coherence Ratio）”指标来量化类别划分的结构特征。研究使用 FineWeb-10BT 数据集合成了 5,872 对 QA，涵盖问题复杂度、答案类型和语言变化三个维度，并在不同颗粒度水平上进行测试。

Result: 实验发现最优颗粒度因维度而异：问题复杂度更适合细粒度划分，而答案类型和语言变化在中间颗粒度表现最佳。此外，通过相干比指标揭示了不同维度在层次结构上的显著差异。人工评估验证了合成数据的高质量。

Conclusion: HieraRAG 提供了一套可移植的框架和验证指标，能够指导从业者根据具体的 RAG 系统配置，确定最优的评估颗粒度，从而提升评估结果的区分度和可靠性。

Abstract: Evaluating retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems requires benchmarks that capture diverse question characteristics, yet practitioners lack empirical guidance on which dimensions to vary and at what granularity. We present HieraRAG, a hierarchical framework for studying granularity in RAG benchmark construction, defining optimal granularity as the level that maximizes discriminative power (the standard deviation of generation quality across categories) within a given RAG configuration. As a case study, we generate 5,872 synthetic question-answer (QA) pairs from FineWeb-10BT across 3 dimensions (Question Complexity, Answer Type, Linguistic Variation) at 3 granularity levels (2, 4, and 8 categories). With a BM25+Falcon-3-10B pipeline, optimal granularity varies by dimension: complexity benefits from fine-grained distinctions (discriminative power: 0.053) while answer type and linguistic variation peak at medium granularity. We introduce a Coherence Ratio metric to quantify whether fine-grained splits cleanly subdivide parent categories, revealing structural differences across dimensions (Question Complexity: 0.40 vs. Answer Type: 1.44). Human evaluation of 110 stratified QA pairs confirms synthetic quality. While these specific findings reflect a single configuration, HieraRAG provides a portable procedure and validation metric for practitioners to determine evaluation granularity within their own RAG settings.

</details>


### [7] [MentalMARBERT: Domain-Adaptive Pre-training and Two-Stage Fine-Tuning for Arabic Mental Health Disorders Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12649)
*Fatimah Almalki,Areej Alhothali,Lulwah Alharigy,Abdulrahman Aladeem*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种两阶段框架，通过领域自适应预训练和分层分类架构，显著提升了阿拉伯语社交媒体文本中心理健康障碍的分类效果，并发布了一个大规模的高质量阿拉伯语心理健康数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阿拉伯语社交媒体文本存在方言多样性、语言非正式、高质量标注资源稀缺以及类严重不平衡等问题，导致针对阿拉伯语心理健康障碍的多分类研究进展缓慢，亟需提升分类准确性和模型泛化能力。

Method: 1. 构建了一个包含50,670条阿拉伯语推文的心理健康数据集；2. 实施两阶段框架：第一阶段对AraBERT、CAMeLBERT和MARBERT进行领域及任务自适应预训练（DAPT和TAPT）；第二阶段对比评估单阶段与分层两阶段架构，并结合全参数微调与LoRA技术。

Result: 研究构建的数据集一致性良好（Krippendorff's Alpha=0.733）；领域自适应后的MARBERT（即MentalMARBERT）性能最优；采用分层两阶段架构结合全参数微调取得了最佳效果，宏观F1值达到0.861，准确率达到0.877。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了领域自适应预训练（DAPT/TAPT）和分层分类架构在解决阿拉伯语心理健康文本分类任务中的有效性。通过构建高质量数据集并优化模型架构，该方法能够显著提升对多种心理健康障碍的分类精度，为阿拉伯语心理健康自然语言处理提供了有力支持。

Abstract: Detecting mental health disorders from Arabic social media text remains challenging due to dialectal variation, informal language, limited high-quality annotated resources, and severe class imbalance. While English mental health natural language processing (NLP) has progressed substantially, Arabic multi-class disorder classification remains insufficiently studied. This study proposes a two-phase framework for Arabic mental health text classification. In phase 1, three Arabic pre-trained language models, AraBERT, CAMeLBERT, and MARBERT, undergo Domain-Adaptive and Task-Adaptive Pretraining (DAPT and TAPT) using a large-scale corpus of unlabeled Arabic mental health tweets. The adapted models are evaluated under a unified protocol to identify the most effective backbone model. In phase 2, the selected model is assessed across four configurations combining single-stage and hierarchical two-stage classification architectures with full fine-tuning and Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA). To support this study, we constructed a novel annotated Arabic mental health dataset comprising 50,670 tweets across six categories, with strong inter annotator agreement (Krippendorff's Alpha = 0.733, average pairwise agreement = 0.797). Experimental results show that the domain-adapted MARBERT (MentalMARBERT) achieves statistically significant improvements over baseline models in both accuracy and macro-F1. The hierarchical two-stage architecture combined with full fine-tuning achieves the best overall performance, reaching a macro-F1 of 0.861 and an accuracy of 0.877. These findings demonstrate the effectiveness of domain-specific adaptive pretraining and hierarchical classification for Arabic mental health disorder detection.

</details>


### [8] [Observable Patterns Are Not Explanations: A Causal-Geometric Analysis of Latent Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12689)
*Darpan Aswal,Thomas Palmeira Ferraz,Yongxin Zhou,Maxime Peyrard*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过实验证明，现有的潜推理模型（LRM）中观察到的“推理模式”并不等同于其实际的推理机制。研究建议应将潜状态视为“隐式计算”而非“隐式解释”，并呼吁在模型可解释性研究中引入严格的对照组和因果推断方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的潜推理模型研究倾向于将观察到的潜状态模式（如类似广度优先搜索的边界或算术计算过程）作为模型内部具备推理机制的证据，但这些现象是否真正驱动了模型的推理行为尚不明确。因此，本研究旨在验证这些潜状态模式是否是真正的推理机制，还是仅仅是模型训练出的伴随现象。

Method: 研究通过对比评估两种代表性LRM（Coconut和CODI）与其去除了循环或课程学习设计的控制模型，分析了潜状态模式的普适性；利用因果干预技术（Causal Interventions）量化潜思维对模型行为的影响程度；并结合几何分析（Geometric Analysis）探讨了潜思维在低秩空间中的演化规律。

Result: 研究发现：1. 所谓的推理模式在缺乏相应结构的控制模型中依然存在，说明其并非推理的充分证据；2. 潜思维对模型行为的影响并非二元存在，而是表现为随因果效力强弱而变化的梯度关系；3. 模型行为的因果影响集中在特定的低秩方向上，随着这些方向对行为影响力的增加，其内部几何结构变得更加有序。

Conclusion: 隐式推理模型（LRM）中的潜变量思维不能被简单地视为“隐式解释”。仅仅依赖可解码性、注意力模式或静态结构无法证明其内部推理机制的存在。对LRM的可解释性研究必须结合匹配的对照组实验和因果干预测试，才能客观评估模型行为背后的真实计算过程。

Abstract: Latent reasoning models (LRMs) replace explicit chain-of-thought with continuous thoughts. Recent work treats observable latent-state patterns, such as BFS-like frontiers and decodable arithmetic computation, as evidence for internal reasoning mechanisms. Evaluating two LRMs (Coconut and CODI) against controls lacking the proposed recurrence or curriculum, we find these patterns also appear in the controls and do not always causally affect behavior. Causal interventions reveal that latent-thought utilization is not binary but graded, scaling with a thought's causal effect on model behavior. Geometric analyses reveal this effect concentrates in low-rank directions whose step-to-step geometry grows more structured as their behavioral influence increases. Latent thoughts should therefore be treated as hidden computation, not hidden explanation: decodability, attention, or static structure alone cannot establish mechanism. LRM interpretability thus requires matched controls and causal tests.

</details>


### [9] [AfriSUD: A Dependency Treebank Collection for Evaluating Models on African Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12708)
*Happy Buzaaba,Cheikh Mouhamadou Bamba Dione,David Ifeoluwa Adelani,Sylvain Kahane,Kim Gerdes,Bruno Guillaume,Kevin Guan,Aremu Anuoluwapo,Naome A. Etori,Shamsuddeen Hassan Muhammad,Utitofon Inyang,Peter Nabende,David Sabiiti Bamutura,Andiswa Bukula,Chinedu Uchechukwu,Rooweither Mabuya,Idris Akinade,Christiane Fellbaum*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 为了解决非洲语言在NLP领域的资源匮乏问题，本项目构建了首个大规模非洲语言句法标注语料库AfriSUD，研究发现现有主流模型在处理这些语言时存在显著的语法解析能力差距。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实验结果显示，即使是当前主流的模型，在处理九种非洲语言的词性标注和依存句法分析时也表现出明显的局限性，这表明这些模型在应对非洲语言特有的形态（如粘着语特征）和韵律（如声调）特征方面仍有待提升。

Conclusion: 当前的NLP模型在处理非洲语言时仍存在明显的语法能力鸿沟，现有的主流架构可能无法完全捕捉非洲语言的结构多样性，这强调了开发针对这些语言的特定研究和资源的必要性。

Abstract: Despite their linguistic diversity and global significance, African languages remain underrepresented in research and resources to support NLP. We aim to bridge this gap by introducing AfriSUD, the first large-scale collection of syntactically annotated treebanks for nine diverse African languages spanning major language families and regions across Sub-Saharan Africa. Using the Surface-Syntactic Universal Dependencies (SUD) framework, our community-led effort provides high-quality, native-speaker verified data that capture typological key features such as agglutination and tone. We evaluate a range of models on AfriSUD for part-of-speech tagging and dependency parsing including non-transformer baselines, multilingual pretrained encoders, and LLMs. Our results reveal a significant syntax gap, where models still show clear limitations across the nine languages, suggesting that existing architectures may not fully capture the structural diversity of African-language syntax.

### [10] [Does AI Reviewer See the Full Picture? Attacking and Defending Multimodal Peer Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12716)
*Xinyu Zhao,Rana Muhammad Shahroz Khan,Zhen Xu,Zhen Tan,Tianlong Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PaperGuard 是首个针对 AI 学术同行评审的多模态基准框架，旨在揭示并防御针对科学论文（文本与图表）的特定领域对抗性攻击。研究发现主流 AI 模型在评审任务中极易被操纵，并提供了一套有效的防范策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型（LLM）和多模态模型（MLLM）在科学同行评审中的应用，其面临严重的对抗性操纵风险。当前研究多集中于纯文本，缺乏对图文并茂的科学论文中跨模态攻击的防御研究，且同行评审的攻击具有“特定领域目标”（如恶意篡改分数）的特性，与常规越狱攻击不同，目前尚无成熟的防御机制。

Method: 该研究提出了 PaperGuard 框架，核心包含三部分：(1) 构建了一个涵盖多个科学领域的多模态同行评审数据集；(2) 设计了一套针对文本（如 GCG）和图像（如 PGD）的跨模态攻击套件；(3) 开发了一种基于分块嵌入检索（chunk-based embedding search）的防御方法，通过定位并缓解恶意指令来应对学术论文的长上下文挑战。

Result: 实验表明，当前最先进的 AI 评审模型普遍容易受到攻击。通过 PaperGuard 评估发现，无论是黑盒提示词注入还是白盒图像扰动，都能有效诱导模型产生偏差。研究验证了所提出的基于分块检索的防御机制在缓解此类攻击中的有效性。

Conclusion: PaperGuard 确立了评估 AI 同行评审鲁棒性的基准、协议和防御策略，为实现可信且具备攻击韧性的 AI 辅助学术评审奠定了基础。研究强调了在处理多模态科学论文时，必须防御针对性的领域攻击，而非仅仅关注通用的安全策略。

Abstract: The integration of Large Language Models (LLMs) and Multimodal LLMs (MLLMs) into scientific peer-review workflows introduces novel and significant risks for adversarial manipulation, especially given the multimodal nature of scientific papers where figures, not just text, convey core evidence. This creates a significant gap: current robustness studies on AI peer-review are overwhelmingly text-only. Moreover, the problem is distinct from standard jailbreaking, as a peer-review attack seeks to induce a domain-specific, targeted failure (e.g., "inflate this score") rather than a general safety policy violation, for which no practical defenses exist. To address this, we introduce PaperGuard, the first comprehensive benchmark designed to systematically evaluate and defend AI-generated peer-review against these domain-specific, cross-modal attacks. Our framework is built on three pillars: (1) a new multimodal peer-review dataset spanning multiple scientific domains; (2) a unified suite of attacks, including black-box prompt injections and white-box perturbations, specifically designed to target both text (GCG) and figures (PGD); and (3) a practical defense, motivated by the long-context challenge of academic papers, that uses chunk-based embedding search to efficiently localize and mitigate harmful instructions. Our extensive experiments, conducted across state-of-the-art models, confirm that AI reviewers are pervasively vulnerable. PaperGuard establishes the foundational benchmark, protocols, and actionable defense necessary to pioneer trustworthy, attack-resilient AI-assisted scholarly reviewing.

### [11] [Agent-based models for the evolution of morphological alternation patterns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12748)
*Aravinth Kulanthaivelu,Richard Sproat*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究利用多智能体仿真和基于大语言模型的评估工具，探讨了语言形态学中不规则交替现象的产生与演化机制，发现其主要是社交网络结构与随机传播机制的产物，而非单纯的功能驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究语言中常见的形态学交替现象（如不规则动词的变化）是如何在缺乏交际优势或学习优势的情况下，依然能够跨越世纪或千年持久存在的演化机制。

Method: 1. 构建多智能体仿真系统，模拟词汇变体在不同网络拓扑、扩散模式及采用策略下的传播与固化过程；2. 引入“AI历史语言学家”系统，利用大型语言模型（LLM）评估仿真生成的形态系统与真实语言的相似度；3. 进行三个具体的历史案例研究，测试历史轨迹的敏感性与可能性。

Result: 1. 仿真显示，形态变体可通过社会学习在群体中传播并固化为词法规则；2. 在无标度社交网络和伯努利随机采用策略的条件下，仿真生成的形态系统在“AI历史语言学家”的评估中表现出最高的真实感和合理性；3. 通过案例研究验证了语言演化路径的偶然性。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了形态学交替（如“go/went”）的演化并非源于功能需求，而是社会动力学与随机性共同作用的结果。通过大规模多智能体仿真与AI评估框架，研究证实了无标度网络拓扑结构和随机采用策略对于生成符合自然语言形态特征的模型至关重要，为理解语言演化的偶然性提供了科学视角。

Abstract: Why is the past of English "go" the apparently unrelated "went"? Such alternations are frequent in languages. They neither aid communication nor learnability, yet they can be persistent, surviving over centuries or millennia.
  We present a multi-agent simulation of the emergence of morphological stem and inflection alternations. Alternate forms arise by phonological changes or, as with "go/went", from lexical alternatives associated with a subset of the population. When an agent 'hears' another agent use a novel form for a slot in the paradigm of a word (say, the past tense of go), they will with some probability adopt that form, possibly spreading its use to other slots in the paradigm that shared the same original form. Thus alternative forms can spread through the population and become entrenched as stem or inflectional marker alternants. Unlike many previous computational studies, our system allows for naturalistic lexical forms, realistic phonological rules, lexicons with hundreds or thousands of entries, and agent populations in the tens or hundreds. It supports several network topologies, diffusion patterns and agent adoption policies.
  One issue with such simulations is evaluation: how realistic is the resulting morphology compared to those of real languages? We introduce the AI Historical Linguist, a novel Large Language Model-driven system that models a debate between two historical linguists. We use this to compare a set of real language morphologies, disguised morphologies, and experimentally evolved morphologies. The results suggest that among the factors that favor more plausible morphologies are scale-free social networks and random Bernoulli adoption of forms.
  We also present three case studies modeling attested historical changes, allowing us to test what might have happened if history had been different.
  All code and data are released.

### [12] [LLMs Can Better Capture Human Judgments--With the Right Prompts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12754)
*Danica Dillion,Chen Cecilia Liu,Baihui Wang,Daniele Barolo,Tanmay Rajore,Niket Tandon,Pranathi Ravikumar,Kurt Gray*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究证明，通过简单的提示词策略（如请求分布数据、关注输入场景的清晰度），可以有效弥补大模型在捕捉人类判断力方面的不足，从而实现更好的AI与人类对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对大型语言模型（LLM）被质疑难以捕捉人类判断分布以及在不同措辞下表现不稳定这两大局限性，研究旨在探索简单的提示工程策略是否能够减轻这些缺陷，从而提升AI与人类判断的一致性（AI-human alignment）。

Method: 研究采用了两套数据集：包含144个道德场景的美国代表性样本，以及涵盖32个国家的《国际社会调查项目》中关于家庭与性别角色的38个道德信念。研究主要通过两类提示策略进行改进：一是要求模型报告响应比例和标准差以捕捉分布信息；二是利用人类的困惑度评分（human confusion ratings）来过滤或优化模型输入场景，并验证模型追踪人类困惑感的能力。

Result: 实验结果显示，通过要求模型报告标准差和响应比例，模型能更好地还原人类的响应分布；利用人类困惑度评分确保场景的清晰度，显著提高了模型的一致性；同时发现LLM能够较好地预测人类的变异性（variability），尽管模型对自己错误的自我评估（calibration）表现较差。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，大型语言模型（LLM）捕捉人类判断力的局限性并非不可逾越。通过优化提示词策略（如要求模型输出响应分布及标准差、关注人类对场景的理解度），可以显著提升AI与人类判断的一致性。尽管模型自我校准能力尚存不足，但通过提问方式的改进，能够有效挖掘模型对人类复杂判断逻辑的模拟能力。

Abstract: Are large language models (LLMs) bad at capturing human judgment? Two commonly stated limitations are that LLMs fail to capture full distributions of responses, and that their judgments are unstable across wording variations. We demonstrate simple prompting strategies that mitigate these limitations. Across two datasets--a U.S.-representative set of 144 moral scenarios and 38 moral beliefs from the International Social Survey Programme's Family and Changing Gender Roles module covering 32 countries--we show how simple elicitation techniques help improve AI-human alignment. First, prompting models to report standard deviations and response proportions recovers the full range of human responses better than common strategies. Second, ensuring scenarios are clear to human participants--as reflected in human confusion ratings--boosts model alignment, and LLMs can track human confusion ratings. At the same time, we find that LLMs' estimates of their own error are poorly calibrated, though they can predict human variability relatively well. These results suggest that asking better questions to LLMs can yield better answers.

### [13] [Rigel: Reverse-Engineering the Metal 4.1 Tensor Compute Path on the Apple M4 Max GPU](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12765)
*Ramchand Kumaresan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过逆向工程揭示了 Apple Metal 4.1 `matmul2d` 的黑盒机制，证明其在 M4 Max 上并非硬件加速运算，并为开发者提供了优化该计算路径的实证依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Apple 的 Metal 4.1 技术规范仅记录了接口信息，刻意隐藏了 `matmul2d` 的硬件执行细节（如是否加速、执行位置、累加器精度及数据碎片布局等）。研究旨在揭开这些黑盒特性，为开发者提供底层性能调优依据。

Method: 作者开发了一套名为 Rigel 的微基准测试框架，采用校验和门控和来源追踪技术，在 M4 Max 芯片上对 `matmul2d` 的性能进行实证分析，并通过吞吐量上限分析、与 `simdgroup_matrix` 对比以及功耗归因等手段进行三角测量与验证。

Result: 研究发现 Metal 4.1 的 fp8 (E4M3) `matmul2d` 并非硬件加速而是由 GPU 模拟执行，其吞吐量仅为 fp16 的 0.94 倍，主要起到降低内存占用的作用；证实其运行于 GPU 着色器而非专用神经引擎；重构了未公开的 8x8 数据碎片布局；并证明手动融合算子可实现 6.5-12.9% 的性能提升。

Conclusion: Rigel 的研究揭示了 Apple Metal 4.1 中 `matmul2d` 的底层运作机制。研究表明该特性在 M4 Max 芯片上并非由专用硬件加速，而是通过 GPU 通用着色器执行。开发者应意识到当前该 API 主要提供内存节省而非计算吞吐量优势，并可通过手动优化算子融合来提升性能。

Abstract: Apple's Metal 4.1 exposes a tensor compute path: the Metal Performance Primitives (MPP) matmul2d operation over cooperative_tensor fragments, whose interface is documented but whose hardware behavior is deliberately hidden. The specification states which data-type rows are supported, never whether they are hardware-accelerated, where the operation physically executes, what its accumulator width is, or how it partitions matrix fragments across threads. We present Rigel, an empirical characterization of this path on a single Apple M4 Max (a pre-neural-accelerator generation). Using a checksum-gated, provenance-tracked microbenchmark harness, Rigel recovers eleven facts the v4.1 specification hides or contradicts. The headline finding: the Metal 4.1 fp8 (E4M3) matmul2d is emulated, not accelerated: it sustains 0.94x the throughput of fp16 despite reading half the operand bytes, so on M4 it is a memory-footprint feature, not a performance feature. We further show, via a three-signal triangulation (throughput ceiling, comparison against simdgroup_matrix, and per-rail power attribution), that matmul2d executes entirely on the GPU shader cores with no dedicated matrix datapath and no evidence of Apple Neural Engine routing; that it accumulates in >=fp32; and we reconstruct the opaque 8x8 cooperative_tensor fragment layout Apple documents nowhere. Acting on the characterization, a hand-fused GEMM + bias + GELU kernel beats the decomposed path by +6.5-12.9% in the cache-resident regime. All findings are reproducible from committed MIT-licensed code and per-cell CSVs.

</details>


### [14] [GENIE: A Fine-Grained Measure for Novelty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12790)
*Ramya Namuduri,Manya Wadhwa,Anshun Asher Zheng,Greg Durrett,Junyi Jessy Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大模型在创造力和多样性上的不足，本文提出了一种细粒度评估指标 GENIE，用于量化生成内容在特定任务特征上的创新性，并评估现有提升模型创造力方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的研究主要关注模型是否具备创造力，但忽略了对其生成内容“创新性”来源及其驱动因素的深入分析。同时，传统的整体评估指标（holistic metrics）难以捕捉创新性的高维特征，也无法解释模型在哪些具体属性上表现出或缺乏新颖性。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为 GENIE 的评估指标。该指标通过分析任务特定的特征，将生成内容的“创新性”置于一组响应的背景下进行量化对比，从而实现对模型生成内容细粒度的评估。

Result: 研究发现，与传统的整体评估指标相比，GENIE 能够有效捕捉创新性的高维特征，并明确指出模型在哪些属性上实现了创新。此外，通过 GENIE 评估发现，现有的缓解方法在提升生成内容创新性方面仍存在局限。

Conclusion: GENIE 提供了一种细粒度的评估框架，能够有效剖析大模型生成内容的创新性来源，并揭示现有提升创造力方法的局限性与改进方向。

Abstract: Large Language Models have consistently demonstrated a lack of creativity and diversity across tasks. Prior work has focused on addressing whether models are capable of generating creative outputs. Here, we aim to consider novelty and investigate what makes model-generated content novel or not novel in a task-specific manner. We propose a fine-grained evaluation metric GENIE to measure the novelty of responses along task-specific features with respect to a population of responses. We show that unlike GENIE, holistic metrics struggle to capture the high-dimensionality of novelty and do not provide insight on which properties they target. Finally, we use GENIE to measure the effectiveness of mitigation methods that address creativity to better understand where these methods can improve novelty.

### [15] [Detect, Remask, Repair: Diffusion Editing for Faithful Summarization of Evolving Contexts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12807)
*Hao Zou,Zachary Horvitz,Chandhru Karthick,Zhou Yu,Kathleen McKeown*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对事件演进导致的摘要过时问题，本文提出了一种基于扩散模型的局部修复框架，通过仅更新摘要中过时的片段而非全量重写，实现了高效、可控且忠实度更高的摘要更新。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界的事件不断演进，导致原有的摘要变得过时。传统的全量重写方法不仅计算开销大，且容易丢弃原有摘要中仍然准确的信息，也无法有效体现信息的变化。因此，研究者旨在探索一种“局部忠实度修复”方法，在保留原有正确内容的前提下，仅对过时部分进行精准更新。

Method: 提出了一种名为 DETECT-REMASK-REPAIR 的扩散模型框架。该方法首先检测摘要中过时或不准确的片段，随后对这些特定区域进行掩码处理，最后利用掩码扩散语言模型进行局部修复。此外，作者还引入了 StreamSum 基准测试集，用于评估在不断演进的事件流背景下的摘要忠实度。

Result: 实验结果表明，该框架在 DialogSum 和 StreamSum 数据集上表现优异。相比全量重写，该方法在保持忠实度的同时，将修复成本降低至 0.5 秒以内。此外，该框架还能作为后处理步骤，提升自回归模型生成摘要的忠实度，并实现了在忠实度、计算速度和内容保留之间的灵活权衡。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了基于掩码扩散模型的局部忠实度修复框架是全量重写的一种高效且可控的替代方案。通过局部修复而非重写，该方法不仅降低了计算成本，还能够明确指出并修正事实性错误，为实时演进的摘要任务提供了新的解决思路。

Abstract: Summaries of real-world events can become outdated as contexts evolve and new information arrives. A common response is to generate a new summary from the updated context, but full regeneration discards the previous draft, can obscure what changed, and may be unnecessary when only a few claims are unsupported. We study localized faithfulness repair: updating outdated spans in an existing summary while preserving supported content. We propose DETECT-REMASK-REPAIR, a diffusion-based framework that identifies, remasks, and repairs outdated regions with masked diffusion language models. To evaluate evolving-context summarization, we introduce StreamSum, a benchmark of synthetic event timelines. Experiments on DialogSum and StreamSum show that localized diffusion repair provides a controllable alternative to full rewriting: faithfulness-steered repair improves early drafts, one-step repair reduces repair cost to under half a second, with the framework enabling faithfulness-speed-preservation tradeoffs across datasets. We also find that the framework can provide a post-hoc correction step that improves faithfulness for autoregressive systems.

</details>


### [16] [Localizing Anchoring Pathways in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12818)
*Hillary N. Owusu,Sarah Wiegreffe,Naomi H. Feldman*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过电路定位技术揭示了大型语言模型中数值锚定效应的内部神经通路，发现该效应在模型内部拥有特定的电路结构，且会随着模型微调而发生演变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型在数值推理任务中容易受到提示词中无关数字的影响，产生认知心理学中的“锚定效应”。研究旨在探索这种锚定敏感信号在模型内部是如何被表征和加工的，以弥补当前对大型语言模型认知偏差内部机制理解的空白。

Method: 研究者采用了受控的多项选择任务范式，定义了“logit差值指标”来量化行为上的锚定效应；并利用基于归因（attribution-based）的电路定位方法，对7B-8B规模的Qwen和Llama系列模型（包括基础版和指令微调版）进行了边级（edge-level）与节点级（node-level）的分析，以定位处理锚定信号的神经网络电路。

Result: 实验发现：1. 边级归因方法比节点级方法更准确地捕捉锚定信号；2. 低锚点和高锚点对应的电路在模型内部具有高度的迁移性，表明锚定处理存在共享的通路结构；3. 基础模型与指令微调模型之间的电路迁移表现出稀疏性，说明后训练过程（post-training）重构了模型处理此类信号的关键路径。

Conclusion: 该研究通过机制可解释性手段揭示了大型语言模型中锚定效应的内部表征机制，证明了这种认知偏差在模型内部有特定的电路结构支持，并指出模型后训练过程会显著改变这些关键通路。

Abstract: Irrelevant numbers in a prompt can shift language model judgments, producing anchoring effects in numerical reasoning. We study where this anchor-sensitive signal is carried inside language models using a controlled multiple-choice setup with shared answer options. We define a logit-difference metric comparing the correct answer option with the answer option corresponding to the anchor, and validate that it tracks behavioral anchoring. Using attribution-based circuit localization on 7B--8B Qwen and Llama base and instruction-tuned models, we find that edge-level methods recover this signal more faithfully than node-level methods. Low- and high-anchor circuits transfer strongly within a model, suggesting shared pathway structure across anchor direction. However, sparse transfer across base and instruction-tuned variants is less reliable, indicating that post-training changes which pathways matter most. Overall, our results provide a mechanistic account of how anchoring-related decision signals are carried inside language models.

### [17] [LoHoSearch: Benchmarking Long-Horizon Search Agents Beyond the Human Difficulty Ceiling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12837)
*Jiarui Zhao,Rongzhi Zhang,Lingchuan Liu,Hao Yang,Xunliang Cai,Xi Su*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对现有搜索智能体基准趋于饱和且难度受限的问题，本文提出了基于知识图谱自动构建的高难度基准 LoHoSearch，实验表明当前先进模型在面对长程复杂搜索任务时表现仍有巨大提升空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的搜索智能体基准（如 BrowseComp）已趋于饱和，且大多由人工编写，存在搜索空间小、结构复杂度低以及缺乏全局统计视角的问题，导致模型性能达到瓶颈，难以准确评估其长程推理能力。

Method: 构建了 LoHoSearch 基准，该基准通过自动化流水线开发，利用包含超过 700 万个维基百科实体的知识图谱，选择具有大规模搜索空间的关系，并将其组装成结构复杂且具有知识图谱验证唯一答案的问题。包含 11 个领域共 544 个经人工验证的问题。

Result: 即使是当前最强大的模型，在 LoHoSearch 上的准确率也仅为 34.74%；现有的上下文管理策略在提升性能方面效果有限（仅提升 6.8%），远低于其在传统基准上的表现。

Conclusion: LoHoSearch 为评估搜索智能体的长程推理与上下文管理能力提供了一个更具挑战性的高难度基准，揭示了当前模型在处理复杂、长链路任务时的显著局限性。

Abstract: Search agent benchmarks exemplified by BrowseComp have rapidly saturated over the past year, with the strongest models surpassing 90% accuracy. Since these benchmarks are predominantly human-authored, annotators lack a global perspective on entity statistics and cannot systematically maximize search space size and structural complexity. This creates a difficulty ceiling that is hard to break. To address this, we introduce LoHoSearch (Long-Horizon Search Agents), a challenging benchmark comprising 544 human-verified questions across 11 domains. LoHoSearch is constructed via an automated pipeline built upon a knowledge graph covering over 7 million Wikipedia entities, which selects relations with large search spaces and assembles them into structurally complex questions with KG-verified unique answers. Our evaluation demonstrates that even the strongest model achieves only 34.74% accuracy, and existing context management strategies (best +6.8%) yield far smaller gains than on prior benchmarks. LoHoSearch provides a more demanding standard for evaluating long-horizon reasoning and context management in search agents.

Abstract: Large Language Models such as GPT-4o and GPT-5 achieve strong zero-shot performance on biomedical claim verification, but cost and opacity limit scalable use. We fine-tune three small LLMs: Phi-3-mini (3.8B), Qwen2.5-3B, and Mistral-7B, via QLoRA on SciFact and HealthVer, providing the first study of QLoRA models against GPT-4o and fine-tuned BioLinkBERT encoders. Mistral-7B QLoRA surpasses both GPT-4o and GPT-5 (up to 12% F1 gain) at a fractional cost using just 1,008 training examples. We conduct extensive in-domain and cross-domain evaluation: models trained on SciFact tested on HealthVer and vice versa, at matched sizes to isolate dataset structure from data quantity. We identify a previously unreported structural artifact in SciFact that inflates in-domain scores, and show through bidirectional out-of-domain evaluation that training on structurally sound data enables robust cross-domain transfer. We plan to release all code and adapter checkpoints.

### [20] [SafeLLM: Extraction as a Hallucination-Resistant Alternative to Rewriting in Safety-Critical Settings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12897)
*Julia Ive,Felix Jozsa,Evridiki Georgaki,Nabeel Sheikh,Emma Cattell,Nick Jackson,Paulina Bondaronek,Ciaran Scott Hill,Richard Dobson*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对医疗合规领域，该研究证明了基于行号的“抽取式RAG”比基于自由文本生成的“重写式RAG”更安全、更准确，且能有效减少幻觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于自由文本重写的RAG系统在处理SOP（标准操作程序）和HR政策等关键文档时，容易产生幻觉且难以在完整性与简洁性之间取得平衡，这对医疗和合规性场景构成了严重挑战，因此需要研究抗幻觉的抽取式替代方案。

Method: 研究对比了多种提示词工程策略，包括行号选定、带安全标注的句子抽取以及多阶段细化流水线。实验使用了NHS（英国国家医疗服务体系）和NICE的各类医疗指南文档，并在不同规模的大语言模型上进行了自动指标评估与专家人工评估。

Result: 行号选定策略表现最优，在大小模型中均保持了极高的术语召回率（高达95%）且幻觉更少。相比之下，虽然安全导向方法提高了精确度，但会导致明显的遗漏；文档结构的差异会显著影响策略效果，协议类文档更适合行号提取，而冗长文档则适合其他策略。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在医疗合规等关键领域，直接基于“行号（line-number）”的抽取式方法优于重写式RAG，能够以更低的幻觉风险实现高召回率。此外，应根据文档结构的复杂程度选择不同的信息提取策略。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to access organisational documentation, including standard operating procedures (SOPs), HR policies and institutional guidelines. However, retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems that rely on free-form rewriting can introduce hallucinations and unstable trade-offs between completeness and conciseness, particularly in safety- and compliance-critical settings. Objectives: To evaluate extraction as a hallucination-resistant alternative to rewriting-based RAG and compare strategies that balance precision, recall and safety across document types and model scales. Methods: We compare multiple prompting strategies, including line-number-based source selection, extraction of relevant guideline sentences with explicit safety annotations, and a multi-stage pipeline that refines draft answers using supporting evidence from source guidelines. Experiments are conducted on documents of varying length and structure, including local NHS acute care and oncology guidelines and UK-wide NICE guidelines, using both frontier-scale and locally deployable models. Performance is assessed using automatic metrics and human expert evaluation of relevance and completeness. Results: Line-number selection achieves the strongest results, outperforming direct copying and safety-focused strategies across both large and small models while maintaining high term recall (up to 95%) and close alignment with source text. Safety-oriented approaches improve precision but introduce systematic omissions, while multi-stage filtering further amplifies this trade-off. Performance varies with document structure: line-based extraction excels in protocol-like content, whereas alternative strategies perform better on more verbose documents (up to 97% term recall).

Method: 提出了一种名为PRISM的多智能体框架，将语音感知、文本响应生成和语音合成拆分为协调的组件。核心创新点包括：1. 引入了“韵律到语言翻译机制”，旨在稳定大语言模型的推理过程；2. 实现了对外部知识工具的按需调用，以增强对话的共情能力与内容准确性。

Result: 实验结果表明，PRISM在共情能力、韵律适配性以及文本响应质量方面均取得了显著提升，且在客观和主观评估指标上表现优于现有基线方法。

Abstract: Empathetic spoken dialogue systems require not only semantically appropriate responses but also emotionally aligned prosodic expression. However, cascade pipelines often discard acoustic cues during speech-to-text conversion, while end-to-end speech models lack interpretable control over emotion and knowledge integration. To address these challenges, we propose PRISM, a multi-agent framework for empathetic spoken dialogue that decouples speech perception, response generation, and speech synthesis into coordinated components. PRISM introduces a prosody-to-language translation mechanism to stabilize large language model reasoning and enables on-demand invocation of external knowledge tools for empathetic dialogue generation. Experimental results demonstrate that PRISM achieves consistent improvements in empathy, prosodic appropriateness, and text response generation quality across objective and subjective metrics. Our code is available at: https://github.com/Bxzfrm/PRISM.

### [22] [X-MADAM-RAG: Diagnosing and Handling Chinese-English Evidence Conflict in Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12903)
*Yongqi Kang,Yu Fu,Yong Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了 RAG 系统在处理多语言冲突证据时的挑战，通过构建 X-RAMDocs-ZHEN 基准和 X-MADAM-RAG 框架发现，虽然模型在模板化任务中表现出色，但在去除模板后的自然语言场景下，文档级信息抽取能力仍是亟待攻克的瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决检索增强生成（RAG）系统在面对互斥或矛盾证据时（尤其在多语言场景下）的性能退化问题，研究模型在受控环境下对冲突证据的处理能力与局限。

Method: 构建了名为 X-RAMDocs-ZHEN 的中英文受控基准测试，涵盖六种证据冲突条件；设计了 X-MADAM-RAG 流水线，通过候选提取、证据修复、候选分组及冲突感知聚合来处理多文档冲突；并开发了去除模板依赖的“自然化压力测试”以评估模型的泛化能力。

Result: 在受控基准上，X-MADAM-RAG 表现优异（严格准确率 0.9667），但因受控基准存在模板规则，其泛化性存疑；在去除模板的自然化压力测试中，X-MADAM-RAG 准确率大幅下滑至 0.3000，且表现逊于基准模型。

Conclusion: X-RAMDocs-ZHEN 和 X-MADAM-RAG 主要作为诊断受控证据冲突的基准工具，而非解决通用幻觉或自然检索鲁棒性问题的成熟方案。研究揭示了当前模型在处理非模板化证据抽取时的脆弱性，文档级抽取能力仍是主要的技术瓶颈。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems may receive evidence that is not merely noisy but mutually contradictory. This issue becomes particularly salient in multilingual settings, where retrieved Chinese and English evidence may support incompatible answer candidates. We study this problem through X-RAMDocs-ZHEN, a controlled Chinese-English benchmark derived from RAMDocs for diagnosing evidence conflict in RAG. The benchmark contains 300 examples across six balanced conditions, including monolingual support, bilingual agreement, reversed conflict directions, and conflict with optional noise. We further examine X-MADAM-RAG, an interpretable pipeline that decomposes evidence handling into per-document candidate extraction, visible-evidence repair, deterministic candidate grouping, and conflict-aware aggregation. On the original controlled benchmark with Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct, X-MADAM-RAG achieves 0.9667 strict accuracy and 0.9767 conflict-aware success, outperforming an evidence-normalized single-call baseline. However, a zero-call rule-only extractor reaches 1.0000 on the same benchmark, revealing strong template regularity. To probe this limitation, we construct a deterministic naturalized stress test that removes explicit answer templates while preserving candidate strings. On its 100-sample subset, rule-only extraction falls to 0.0000, but X-MADAM-RAG also drops to 0.3000 strict accuracy, below both naive and evidence-normalized baselines. A privileged oracle remains perfect, indicating that document-level extraction is the main bottleneck. These findings position X-RAMDocs-ZHEN and X-MADAM-RAG as diagnostic tools for controlled evidence conflict rather than as evidence of general hallucination detection or robustness to natural retrieval.

### [23] [SENTINEL: Failure-Driven Reinforcement Learning for Training Tool-Using Language Model Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12908)
*Ziyi Wang,Yuxuan Lu,Yimeng Zhang,Qun Liu,Chen Luo,Jiri Gesi,Hanqing Lu,Yisi Sang,Manling Li,Jing Huang,Dakuo Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SENTINEL是一种新型失败驱动强化学习框架，通过分析模型执行任务时的失败轨迹，自动生成针对性的难点训练任务，从而更高效地提升语言模型代理工具使用的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现有的强化学习训练中，任务分布往往在训练前固定，导致模型在训练后期因任务难度与能力不匹配而产生大量无效的“学习回放（rollouts）”，限制了工具使用代理性能的提升。

Method: 提出了名为SENTINEL的“失败驱动”强化学习框架。该框架包含三个核心组件：控制器（Controller）负责分析失败轨迹并总结错误模式；提案器（Proposer）根据错误模式生成具有针对性的可执行任务；求解器（Solver）则在这些针对性任务上进行强化学习训练，从而实现闭环优化。

Result: 在Tau2-Bench Retail基准测试中使用Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507模型进行评估，SENTINEL将Pass@1准确率从66.4提升至74.9，并在各类通用合成任务的Pass@k指标上优于传统强化学习方法。

Conclusion: 该研究证实，利用模型失败案例作为训练信号是一种有效且可扩展的方法，能够显著增强语言模型代理在使用工具时的可靠性和任务处理能力。

Abstract: Language model agents are increasingly effective in solving realistic tasks through multi-turn tool use. However, training reliable tool-using agents remains challenging in practice. While reinforcement learning provides an on-policy paradigm for improving agents from their own environment interactions, its effectiveness depends heavily on the training task distribution. When tasks are fixed before training, the task distribution can become increasingly mismatched with the policy's evolving capabilities, causing many rollouts to be spent on uninformative tasks. We propose SENTINEL, a failure-driven reinforcement learning framework that turns the Solver's rollout failures into targeted training tasks. SENTINEL follows a Controller--Proposer--Solver loop: the Controller analyzes failed trajectories and summarizes recurring error patterns, the Proposer generates executable tasks that stress these weaknesses, and the Solver is trained on the targeted tasks. On Tau2-Bench Retail with Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507, SENTINEL improves Pass\^{}1 from 66.4 to 74.9 and outperforms RL on general synthetic tasks across Pass\^{}k metrics. These results demonstrate that model failures provide an effective and scalable source of targeted training signal for improving tool-using language model agents.

</details>


### [24] [PiDA: Phonetically-Informed Data Augmentation for Robust Vietnamese Speech Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12911)
*Giang Son Nguyen,Tung X. Nguyen,Hieu Minh Truong,Nhu Vo,Wray Buntine,Dung D. Le*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文针对越南语级联语音翻译中的ASR错误传播问题，提出了一种基于语音相似性的数据增强方法（PiDA），显著提升了系统对错误转录的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 级联式语音翻译系统在处理错误的ASR转录时，存在严重的错误传播问题，导致翻译性能下降。研究者希望通过深入分析ASR错误的语音成因，利用这些发现缓解错误传播带来的影响。

Method: 1. 对越南语语音翻译中的ASR错误进行了首次系统化分类，按语音成因分类替代错误；2. 使用线性混合效应模型（Linear Mixed-Effects Modelling）量化ASR错误对下游神经机器翻译（NMT）性能的影响；3. 提出“语音感知数据增强”（PiDA）：利用语音词嵌入，通过替换为发音相似的词来生成类似ASR的错误样本，并以此对模型进行微调。

Result: 研究发现，越南语ASR替代错误主要由语音相似性引起；使用PiDA方法在FLEURS数据集上进行微调后，系统在处理有瑕疵的ASR输出时，BLEU分数最高提升了2.04点，且对干净文本的翻译质量也有小幅改善。

Conclusion: 研究证实了语音识别（ASR）中的替代错误主要源于语音混淆而非随机噪声，这些错误对级联语音翻译质量有显著负面影响。提出的PiDA方法通过引入针对性的语音感知数据增强，有效提升了模型对错误ASR输出的鲁棒性，并在提升翻译性能的同时保持了对干净文本的良好处理能力。

Abstract: Cascaded speech translation (ST) systems suffer from error propagation when Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) outputs incorrect transcripts. We present the first systematic categorization of ASR errors for Vietnamese ST, classifying substitution errors by phonetic cause and quantifying their impact on downstream Neural Machine Translation (NMT) performance using Linear Mixed-Effects Modelling. We confirm that most ASR substitution errors arise from phonetic confusions rather than random noise, and that these phonetic errors significantly degrade ST quality. Motivated by this finding, we propose Phonetically-Informed Data Augmentation (PiDA), which generates ASR-like corruptions by substituting words with phonetically similar alternatives using phonetic word embeddings. Fine-tuning on a PiDA-augmented version of FLEURS Vietnamese-English improves translation of erroneous ASR outputs (up to +2.04 BLEU over standard fine-tuning) while also slightly improving clean-text performance.

### [25] [Polar: A Benchmark for Evaluating Political Bias in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12922)
*Sangho Kim,Heejin Kim,Yoonhee Park,Hyunggeun Jeon,Jaejin Lee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个多语言、多语境的政治偏见基准测试“Polar”，揭示了大语言模型的政治偏见并非固定，而是随着政治语境、议题类别和语言输入发生系统性变化，呼吁进行更广泛的跨文化模型评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型中的政治偏见问题日益突出，但目前缺乏一种能够跨语言和跨政治语境进行可重复测量的标准评估方法。研究旨在填补这一空白，深入探讨政治偏见在不同模型、议题、语言和地缘政治背景下的表现差异。

Method: 研究引入了一个名为“Polar”的基准测试，包含4,026个多选题。不同于传统的提示词生成评估，该方法通过测量模型对不同选项的概率分布（likelihoods）来评估偏见。基准涵盖了两个意识形态轴和八个议题类别（基于Manifesto Project），并在美国和韩国的政治语境下进行了平行评估，同时测试了语言翻译对偏见的影响。

Result: 研究发现，38个大语言模型的政治偏见呈现系统性差异。在美国政治内容上，所有模型均表现出左翼进步倾向；而在韩国语境下，模型表现则更为中立和混合。此外，实验证实仅改变呈现语言就能改变模型的测量偏见，证明了偏见的评价具有语境依赖性。

Conclusion: 该研究强调了政治偏见评估不能仅依赖单一语言或特定文化背景。为了构建更具包容性和公平性的模型，必须在多语言和跨文化语境下对大语言模型进行系统性的偏见评估，因为偏见不仅受模型训练的影响，还受到呈现语言和上下文的显著干扰。

Abstract: Political bias in large language models (LLMs) is increasingly significant, but difficult to measure reproducibly across political and linguistic contexts. We introduce Polar, a 4,026-instance multiple-choice benchmark that measures political bias through option-level likelihoods rather than prompt-based generation. Polar covers two ideological axes and eight issue categories derived from the Manifesto Project, and evaluates models in parallel across U.S. and South Korean political contexts. Across 38 LLMs, measured bias varies systematically with political context, issue category, model group, and presentation language. All models lean left-progressive on U.S. political content, but show more centered and mixed patterns on South Korean content. Translation experiments further show that presentation language alone can shift measured bias. These findings highlight the need for multilingual and cross-contextual evaluation of political bias in LLMs.

### [26] [Multi-Turn Reasoning When Context Arrives in Pieces: Scalable Sharding and Memory-Augmented RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12941)
*Shu Tong Luo,Wenqin Liu,Rui Liu,Mingming Gong,Jiaxian Guo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过训练模型维护滚动记忆的方法，解决了大模型在处理多轮对话时的信息丢失问题，并利用自动分片技术实现了高效训练，显著提升了模型的增量推理与泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究人员发现大语言模型（LLM）在跨多轮对话处理关键任务信息时，准确率会大幅下降（高达65%），即便模型具备完整的上下文信息。为了解决这种“对话中迷失”（Lost in Conversation）现象，需要一种更有效的上下文处理策略。

Method: 引入一种低成本的分片管道（sharding pipeline），将单轮QA数据集自动转化为多轮碎片化信息片段，以此训练模型维护一个紧凑的滚动记忆（rolling memory），而非依赖于不断增长的对话历史。

Result: 基于GSM8K数据集的训练实验表明，该记忆增强策略显著提升了多轮对话的准确率，实现了在更难数学题和领域外长上下文QA任务上的零样本泛化，且在测试阶段即使提供完整历史，其表现也优于传统的完整历史基准模型。

Conclusion: 学习压缩信息不仅能有效解决长对话中的信息丢失问题，还能诱导模型产生更稳健的增量推理能力，且这种能力具有跨任务和跨领域泛化性。

Abstract: When a user reveals task-critical information across several conversation turns, LLM accuracy drops by up to 65% despite full context availability. We show that this Lost in Conversation degradation can be substantially mitigated by training models to maintain a compact rolling memory instead of attending to a growing history. To make such training scalable, we introduce a low-cost sharding pipeline that converts single-turn QA datasets into multi-turn fragmented-information episodes, eliminating the need for hours of manual annotation. Training only on sharded GSM8K, our memory-augmented policy significantly improves multi-turn accuracy and generalises zero-shot to harder math and out-of-domain long-context QA. Moreover, memory-trained models outperform full-history baselines even when given the full history at test time, suggesting that learning to compress induces more robust incremental reasoning than full-context exposure alone.

### [27] [SkillChain: Closing the Loop on Skill Evolution for Image-Based E-Commerce AI Assistants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12984)
*Yimin Hu,Mengtao Xu,Hao Guo,Yuheng Song,Xiaoyong Zhu,Bo Zheng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对电商 AI 助手意图复杂多变的问题，本文提出了 SkillChain 系统，通过自动化生命周期管理（创建、路由、优化）实现了技能的高效演化，显著提升了生产环境下的服务质量与用户指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电商平台上的 AI 图像助手需要处理多种异构意图（如搜索、推荐、百科等），现有大语言模型系统难以在没有明确行为约束的情况下满足不同领域的高质量标准，且手动工程化扩展意图空间不可行。

Method: SkillChain 包含三个核心阶段：1. Skill Creator：根据任务规范和轨迹进行技能引导；2. Route Optimizer：负责意图路由对齐；3. Body Refiner：通过双路径 LLM-Judge 评估机制进行迭代式的技能体优化。

Result: 在生产级电商图像助手上的部署显示，SkillChain 显著提升了响应质量（结构合规性和内容质量）。在线 A/B 测试证实，该系统有效提升了用户参与度、内容消费及长期留存率。

Conclusion: SkillChain 提出了一种自动化、可扩展的系统，能够有效解决电商领域复杂多变的 AI 视觉助理意图处理问题，并通过闭环反馈机制显著提升了用户体验与业务指标。

Abstract: Image-based AI assistants are now deployed at production scale on e-commerce platforms, where a single uploaded image can trigger fundamentally different user intents: product search, style recommendation, visual encyclopedia, or utility tool calls, each demanding its own response format, tool invocation, and domain knowledge. Without per-intent behavioral constraints, LLM-based systems conflate these heterogeneous modes and fall short of domain quality standards, while the breadth and dynamism of the intent space render manual engineering infeasible. To address this, we present SkillChain, which closes the production feedback loop on Skill evolution, automating the lifecycle of Skills through three stages: Skill Creator for bootstrapping from task specs and trajectories, Route Optimizer for routing alignment, and Body Refiner for iterative Skill Body refinement via dual-path LLM-Judge evaluation. Deployed on a production-scale e-commerce image assistant, SkillChain substantially improves aggregate response quality, with the strongest gains on structural compliance and content quality; a one-week online A/B experiment further confirms significant gains in user engagement, content consumption, and long-term retention.

### [28] [No Hidden Prompts Needed! You Can Game AI Peer Review with Presentation-Only Revisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13044)
*Xu Yang,Zhizhou Sha,Junbo Li,Jian Yu,Yifan Sun,Matthew Zhao,Jinrui Fang,Xinyue Guo,Yining Wu,Xu Hu,Yifu Luo,Qiang Liu,Zhangyang Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了AI审稿人面临的重大安全隐患：仅通过调整论文的包装方式（如摘要和论述框架），即便不改动任何核心科研内容，也能显著提高AI给出的评分。这一发现表明，AI审稿人过度依赖论文的呈现形式，容易被策略性的叙述所误导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前针对AI审稿人的安全性研究多集中在提示词注入（Prompt Injection）等显性攻击。本研究旨在探讨一种更具现实意义且隐蔽的失败模式：即使没有恶意注入，仅通过优化论文的呈现方式（Packaging），是否就能操纵AI审稿人的评分。研究者希望揭示AI审稿人是否能够真正锚定科学实质，而非被肤浅的文字重构所欺骗。

Method: 研究者提出了一种名为“对抗性重包装”（Adversarial Repackaging）的闭环攻击方法。该方法在保持原始科学内容（如方法、实验数据、证明、公式等）完全不变的前提下，利用AI审稿人的反馈作为引导，迭代地对论文的展示层内容（如摘要、贡献叙述、相关工作引用、讨论结构）进行修改，以实现最优的评估分数。同时，作者构建了一个无污染的滚动基准测试来评估AI审稿人的鲁棒性。

Result: 在针对三种主流AI审稿人的测试中，“对抗性重包装”攻击的成功率高达75.1%，平均评分提升了1.21分（满分10分）。实验表明，该效果并非简单的文本润色所致，而是通过重构相关工作引用和扩展分析讨论来引导审稿人认知。研究发现，AI审稿人更倾向于“被夸大优点所吸引”，而非“被严谨的逻辑所说服”，且容易将“提及局限性”误认为是“解决了局限性”。

Conclusion: AI审稿人的评估极其容易受到论文呈现方式（如摘要和论述框架）的影响，而非仅依赖科学证据。论文包装已成为一种新的优化层面，可能导致对科学价值的误判。未来的AI评审系统必须加强对科学内容与包装策略的区分能力，防止仅仅通过文字润色和框架调整获得虚高评分。

Abstract: As AI-generated reviews move from experimental tools into peer-review infrastructure, most robustness concerns have focused on explicit attacks such as hidden instructions and prompt injection. We study a harder and more policy-relevant failure mode: no hidden text, no prompt injection, and no changes to methods, experiments, figures, equations, proofs, or numerical results. The attacker modifies only presentation-level content, such as the abstract, contribution framing, related work, discussion, and narrative structure. We introduce adversarial repackaging: a closed-loop attack that uses AI-reviewer feedback to search for presentation-level revisions while keeping the scientific evidence fixed. Across three mainstream AI reviewers, adversarial repackaging achieves a 75.1% attack success rate and a mean score gain of +1.21/10. The effect is not explained by ordinary prose polishing. We also reveal that strategies that change how the reviewer interprets the paper, such as related-work repositioning and analytical discussion expansion, substantially outperform surface edits such as local polishing, table formatting, and algorithm boxes.
  Our analysis reveals two deeper structural failure modes. First, AI reviewers are easier to impress than to convince: highlighting strengths reliably increases perceived merit, while attempts to dissolve weaknesses frequently backfire. Second, AI reviewers can confuse the appearance of addressing a limitation with actually resolving it, allowing unchanged evidence to be reinterpreted as stronger scientific contribution. These results show that the deployment risk is not only malicious hidden instructions, but the emergence of paper presentation itself as an optimization surface. We release a contamination-free rolling benchmark and attack framework for testing whether AI reviewers remain anchored to scientific content under presentation-only edits.

</details>

*Katharina Sommer,Tristan Till,Florian Matthes*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于本地部署MedGemma-27B的二阶段架构，通过少样本上下文学习有效解决了临床文档信息提取中的隐私、成本及幻觉问题，在性能上表现优异，为临床NLP提供了安全、高效的替代方案。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种基于MedGemma-27B的二阶段架构：第一阶段进行二进制存在性分类，第二阶段进行数值提取。通过采用基于项目特定的少样本上下文学习（Few-shot ICL），在不进行模型微调或调用外部API的前提下，强制模型严格遵循文本证据，确保输出结果的确定性。

Conclusion: 本研究证实，通过构建完全本地化、隐私保护的LLM管道，可以在不依赖外部API和微调的情况下，实现接近专有大模型的临床信息提取性能，为医疗NLP提供了一种数据主权友好的实用框架。

Abstract: The extraction of structured clinical information from unstructured EHR notes is a persistent bottleneck in healthcare informatics. While large language models (LLMs) offer high performance, their deployment in clinical settings is hindered by privacy risks, inference costs, and the tendency to hallucinate beyond textual evidence. We address these challenges for the CL4Health 2026 Case Report Form (CRF) filling task by proposing a fully local, domain-adapted pipeline using the MedGemma-27B model. Our two-stage architecture, which separates binary presence classification from value extraction, enforces strict adherence to textual evidence and ensures deterministic outputs for negated, uncertain, or unknown states. By leveraging item-specific, few-shot in-context learning without external API calls or fine-tuning, our approach achieves a macro-F1 score of 0.55 on the official English test track. This result secures second place among all locally-hosted, open-source submissions. Our work demonstrates that privacy-preserving, on-premise LLM pipelines can achieve near-competitive performance with proprietary frontier models, providing a practical, data-sovereign framework for clinical NLP.

### [30] [LEDGER: A Long-Context Benchmark of Corporate Annual Reports for Grounded Financial Retrieval and Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13100)
*Charles Moslonka,Amaury de Vitry,Arthur Garnier,Hicham Randrianarivo,Emmanuel Malherbe*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对金融领域长文本处理评估不足的问题，研究发布了LEDGER数据集，包含近5000份完整的企业年度报告及KPI标注，并设立了三项难度递进的评估基准，为大模型在复杂金融文档中的事实检索、信息提取与分析能力提供了严谨的评估标准。

Method: 构建了名为LEDGER的金融数据集，包含4,999份完整的数字化年度报告，并附带31个KPI标注及其与市场反应的关联；设计了三个层次的评估基准：基于页面的KPI检索（TREC风格）、对话式“大海捞针”查询，以及完整的KPI提取任务，并提供配套的OCR标注、验证工具及评分链。

Conclusion: LEDGER数据集通过提供包含图表和叙述的完整年度报告，填补了金融领域长文本评估的空白，为评估大模型在复杂金融文档中的事实提取和推理能力提供了重要工具，并揭示了语言模型在金融领域应用的前景与挑战。

Abstract: Finance reporting is a natural proving ground for large language models, and the very-long-context capabilities of recent models across all sizes make rigorous evaluation in this domain an increasingly pressing need. Yet most public financial resources reduce the task to plain-text SEC 10-K filings paired with a handful of question-answer items. We release LEDGER (Long-context Evaluation of Documents for Grounded Extraction and Retrieval), a corpus of 4,999 digitized corporate annual reports - full documents with figures, tables, and narrative, not just regulatory filings. Each report is labeled with 31 consolidated financial KPIs to be extracted and linked to the market's reaction at the earnings date. From this data we derive three evaluation benchmarks spanning the difficulty spectrum: a pure page-level KPI retrieval task with TREC-style relevance judgments over 118,048 questions in natural language, a conversational "needle-in-a-haystack" single-value lookup, and a full KPI extraction task, both from long, numerically dense reports. We additionally provide human OCR-quality annotations with inter-annotator agreement and the complete extraction, validation, and scoring toolchain. We further demonstrate the dataset's research utility with a case study linking CEO-letter rhetoric to post-publication market impact.

### [31] [MÖVE: A Holistic LLM Benchmark for the German Public Sector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13111)
*Camilla Dalerci,Thilo Michael,Robin Schaefer,Daniel Weinland*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MÖVE 是首个专注于德国公共行政领域的 LLM 基准测试，通过结合性能指标与治理准则（如合规性、能效），为政务场景下的模型选型提供了客观、多维的评估体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LLM 基准测试多以英语和美国场景为主，缺乏对德国公共行政特殊语境（如法律要求、行政流程、德语语料）的针对性评估，导致政务部门在模型选型时缺乏科学指导。

Method: 研究人员构建了涵盖摘要、问答和主题提取的性能指标，以及包含幻觉倾向、能耗、透明度及对德国宪法价值合规性的治理指标。通过使用十个德语数据集（包含自建的公共管理领域数据集），结合传统 NLP 指标、基于嵌入的方法及“LLM-as-a-judge”评估策略对 39 个模型进行了全方位评估。

Result: 评估显示没有单一模型能在所有指标上均领先，模型规模与性能并无直接对应关系。研究揭示了任务表现与治理准则之间的权衡，并验证了基准测试本身的统计稳健性，为政务 AI 选型提供了数据驱动的参考。

Conclusion: MÖVE 是一个针对德国公共部门的动态基准测试，它打破了单一模型统治的观念，强调了在公共管理领域模型选择需权衡任务表现与治理合规性（如隐私、价值观、能效）的重要性，为政务 AI 的可持续发展提供了科学依据。

Abstract: We present MÖVE (Modelle für die Öffentliche Verwaltung Evaluieren), a holistic benchmark for evaluating large language models (LLMs) in the context of the German public sector. While LLMs are increasingly adopted in public administration, model selection remains largely ad hoc, and existing benchmarks offer limited guidance: they are predominantly English-centric, US-centric in content, and focus exclusively on task performance. MÖVE addresses these gaps by evaluating 39 models across two complementary dimensions. Performance criteria cover summarization, question answering, and topic extraction. Governance criteria assess hallucination tendencies, energy consumption, provider transparency, and alignment with German constitutional values and knowledge about positions by German political parties. In total, we utilize ten German-language datasets, including gold- and silverstandard datasets that we constructed to reflect public-administration domains. We employ a multi-metric evaluation strategy combining classical NLP metrics, embedding-based methods, and LLM-as-a-judge approaches. Our results show that no single model dominates across all criteria: top performers differ between tasks, and model size alone is a poor predictor of quality. We further evaluate the benchmark itself, analyzing its statistical precision, LLM judge reliability, the impact of our private datasets on model rankings, the sensitivity of our results to prompt formulation, and the validity of our energy consumption estimates. MÖVE is designed as a living benchmark under active development; results are publicly available at https://moeve.bundesdruckerei.de/.

</details>


### [32] [G-Long: Graph-Enhanced Memory Management for Efficient Long-Term Dialogue Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13115)
*Minjun Choi,Yoonjin Jang,Sangwon Youn,Youngjoong Ko*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: G-Long 是一种高效的长对话记忆管理框架，它利用小模型提取图结构化数据，并通过新型注意力得分机制实现精准记忆检索，在提升对话质量和召回率的同时，大幅降低了计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在长对话系统中面临长上下文推理能力不足、处理原始文本效率低的问题，现有方案要么存在信息丢失（非结构化存储），要么计算成本过高（大规模 LLM），因此需要一种高效且一致的记忆管理框架。

Method: 提出了 G-Long 框架：1. 使用经过微调的小型语言模型（sLM）进行结构化三元组提取，构建知识图谱以存储记忆；2. 引入基于 T5 摘要器交叉注意力信号的“注意力感知重要性评分机制”，用于识别和筛选关键记忆；3. 利用图结构进行关联检索。

Result: G-Long 在多个基准测试中达到了最先进水平：在 MSC 数据集上响应质量提升了 9.8%，在 LME 数据集上检索召回率提升了 40.8%，同时显著降低了计算开销。

Conclusion: G-Long 通过引入图结构化记忆管理和注意力感知的重要性评分机制，成功在长对话系统中实现了低延迟、高精度的长短期记忆维持，证明了结构化知识图谱与小模型结合在处理长上下文任务中的优越性。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) have advanced open-domain dialogue systems, maintaining long-term consistency remains a challenge due to inherent limitations in long-context reasoning and the inefficiency of processing extensive raw text. Existing approaches typically rely on either unstructured memory storage, which is prone to information loss, or computationally expensive LLMs that incur high latency. To address these limitations, we propose G-Long, a graph-enhanced framework that utilizes a fine-tuned small Language Model (sLM) for structured triplet extraction and associative retrieval, significantly reducing operational costs. Furthermore, we introduce the novel attention-aware importance scoring mechanism that leverages the intrinsic cross-attention signals of a T5 summarizer to identify salient memories. Extensive experiments across diverse benchmarks demonstrate that G-Long achieves state-of-the-art performance in both response generation and memory retrieval, yielding performance gains of up to 9.8% in response quality on MSC and 40.8% in retrieval recall on LME, while significantly minimizing computational overhead.

### [33] [EvoBrowseComp: Benchmarking Search Agents on Evolving Knowledge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13120)

Main category: cs.CL

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的搜索智能体评估基准（如 BrowseComp）依赖静态知识，易受测试集污染和参数化记忆影响，导致模型通过事实回忆而非真正的检索与推理来获得高分，无法真实反映其搜索能力。

Method: 提出了一套三智能体协作框架，包含：1. QA 合成智能体，从实时网络检索最新知识生成问答对；2. 信息过滤智能体，筛选高信度与高流行度内容以规避参数化记忆捷径；3. 高层引导智能体，将问题形式化为推理图以减少逻辑冗余。该框架支持全自动化合成，确保基准测试的动态更新。

Result: 构建了包含 400 个英语和 400 个中文问题的 EvoBrowseComp 数据集。实验证明该基准具有极高的难度，强制要求智能体进行广泛的水平搜索，有效地规避了逻辑捷径，展现了良好的抗污染能力与时效性。

Conclusion: EvoBrowseComp 建立了一种可扩展的自动更新基准测试范式，能够有效应对模型能力提升与世界知识不断演变带来的挑战，是评估搜索智能体真实浏览与推理能力的可靠工具。

Existing benchmarks such as BrowseComp rely on static knowledge, making them vulnerable to test-set contamination and parametric memorization. Consequently, models can achieve high scores through fact recall rather than genuine retrieval, obscuring true browsing competence via reasoning shortcuts.
  In this paper, we introduce EvoBrowseComp, an evolving benchmark of 400 English and 400 Chinese contamination-free complex questions synthesized via live-web traversal. To collect these questions, we design a three-agent collaborative framework: (1) a QA synthesis agent that retrieves fresh knowledge from the live web to synthesize QA pairs; (2) an information filtering agent that filters retrieved knowledge in terms of credibility and popularity to block parametric shortcuts; and (3) a high-level guidance agent that formalizes questions into reasoning graphs to reduce logical redundancy and shortcuts in synthesized QA pairs. Because the framework supports fully automated synthesis, EvoBrowseComp can be regularly updated to prevent data contamination and maintain temporal freshness. Extensive experiments confirm its great difficulty, requiring broad horizontal search. It establishes a scalable paradigm for auto-updatable, high-difficulty benchmarking that keeps pace with both evolving world knowledge and advancing agent capabilities.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种流畅度感知的优化框架，该框架利用模型内部信号（如语言多样性和语音持续时间的诱导性时间变异性）来最小化块间停顿，从而在低延迟和自然语流之间寻找平衡点。

To bridge this gap, we introduce a fluency-aware optimization framework designed to discover the sweet spot between the low-latency benefits of simultaneous translation and the natural flow of consecutive translation. Our framework minimizes inter-chunk silences by leveraging model-internal signals, including linguistic diversity and induced temporal variability in speech durations. Experiments on short- and long-form benchmarks show that our framework produces natural speech flow while maintaining competitive latency and translation quality.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于角色的对话系统多将角色描述视为平铺的句子集合，忽略了角色属性之间的高阶语义关系（如共享同一主题类别），导致生成响应的一致性不足。

Method: 提出HyPE（超图角色编码器）框架，包含两个核心步骤：1. 将角色文本解析为“核心、表达、情感、类别”四元组；2. 构建基于类别标签的超图结构，并利用HyperGCN进行信息传递，结合持久化边缘嵌入（PEE）生成角色摘要向量和软记忆库，从而指导响应生成。

Result: 在PersonaChat数据集上，HyPE在GPT-2、LLaMA-3.2-3B及Qwen2.5-3B等多种大模型骨干上，均优于传统的句子级池化基线方法。

Abstract: Persona-grounded dialogue systems aim to produce responses consistent with a speaker's persona, yet existing methods treat personas as a flat set of sentences and fail to model the high-order relations among persona attributes-e.g., that several persona sentences share a topical category. We propose HyPE (Hypergraph Persona Encoder), a framework that (i) analyzes each persona-bearing text as a (Core, Expression, Sentiment, Category) quadruple, and (ii) organizes persona elements into a hypergraph whose hyperedges are induced by shared category labels. An HyperGCN hypergraph neural network propagates this structure into a persona summary vector and a soft-memory bank that condition the response generator. We further propose Persistent Edge Embeddings (PEE), lightweight per-category learnable priors fused into the HyperGCN message-passing step. On PersonaChat under greedy decoding, HyPE consistently outperforms sentence-level pooling baselines across GPT-2, LLaMA-3.2-3B, and Qwen2.5-3B backbones by demonstrating that structured hyperedge-level persona encoding provides a transferable advantage across model scales.

### [36] [NTS-CoT: Mitigating Hallucinations in LLM-based News Timeline Summarization with Chain-of-Thought Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13171)
*Feng Lyu,Huiqin Yan,Sijing Duan,Hao Wu,Shuang Gu,Xue Qiao,Weixu Zhang,Haolun Wu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线新闻更新速度极快，时间线摘要（TLS）需求迫切。然而，当前基于大语言模型（LLM）的 TLS 方法仍存在严重的幻觉问题（如内容不忠实和信息遗漏），且学术界对此缺乏深入研究。

Method: 提出了一种名为 NTS-CoT 的框架，包含三个核心模块：1) Element-CoT：通过提取新闻核心要素确保摘要的忠实度；2) 日期选择模块：结合时间显著性和事件突出性来筛选关键时间戳；3) Causal-CoT：通过推理因果关系以减少时间点事件的遗漏。

Result: 在三个 TLS 基准测试中的定量分析及人工评估结果表明，NTS-CoT 优于现有的前沿基线方法，在显著缓解幻觉问题的同时，提升了整体摘要性能。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的 NTS-CoT 框架有效解决了大语言模型在时间线摘要（TLS）任务中的幻觉问题。通过引入思维链推理，该模型显著提升了摘要的忠实度和完整性，为处理动态新闻流的自动摘要任务提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: The rapid updates of online news make tracking event developments challenging, highlighting the need for timeline summarization (TLS). Hallucinations, where LLM-generated content deviates from source news, still remain a critical issue in LLM-based TLS and are not well studied in existing works. To bridge this gap, we identify two primary types of hallucinations: unfaithful content during news summarization and information omission in date-event summarization. Then, we propose NTS-CoT, a novel framework that leverages Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning to mitigate hallucinations in TLS. The framework consists of three key modules: i) Element-CoT to capture essential news elements for faithful summarization, ii) Date Selection to combine temporal saliency and event prominence for timestamp selection, and iii) Causal-CoT to infer causal relationships and reduce omissions in date-event summarization. Extensive experiments, including quantitative analysis on three TLS benchmarks and human evaluation, demonstrate that NTS-CoT outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, effectively mitigating hallucinations and improving LLM-based TLS performance. ### [37] [MemRefine: LLM-Guided Compression for Long-Term Agent Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13177)
*Minjae Kim,Jinheon Baek,Soyeong Jeong,Sung Ju Hwang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对 LLM 代理长期交互中的记忆无限增长问题，本文提出了 MemRefine 框架，通过 LLM 决策来智能合并与清理冗余记忆，在满足固定存储预算的前提下最大化保留有用信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型（LLM）代理交互时间的延长，记忆库会无限增长并充斥冗余信息，这不仅增加了存储成本，还会干扰有效信息的检索。在资源受限的环境下，如何在固定存储预算内保留未来任务所需的核心信息成为一个亟待解决的问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为 MemRefine 的 LLM 指导框架。该方法首先利用相似度检索候选记忆对，随后由 LLM 作为决策者，基于事实内容执行删除、合并或保留操作，并以迭代方式直至满足设定的存储预算。

Result: 实验结果表明，MemRefine 在多个记忆框架和长期对话基准测试中，能够在严格预算下稳定运行，在保持下游任务性能的同时，表现显著优于基于规则的传统基线方法。

Conclusion: MemRefine 通过引入 LLM 进行语义理解和决策，能够有效地在存储预算限制下管理对话记忆。该方法证实了基于事实价值的记忆精简优于基于表面相似度的规则方法，是解决资源受限环境下长期记忆问题的有效方案。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents are increasingly expected to operate over long-term interactions, where information from past dialogues must be preserved and recalled to support future tasks. However, as interactions accumulate, the memory store grows without bound and fills with redundant entries that inflate storage cost and degrade retrieval by crowding out the most useful evidence. Furthermore, this is especially limiting on resource-constrained platforms with hard memory budgets, motivating us to formulate storage-budgeted memory management, the task of keeping an already constructed memory store within a fixed budget while preserving information useful for future interactions. To this end, we then propose MemRefine, an LLM-guided framework that, since surface similarity poorly reflects factual value, uses similarity only to propose candidate pairs and defers delete, merge, and preserve decisions to an LLM judge based on factual content, iterating until the budget is met. Across multiple memory frameworks and long-term conversation benchmarks, MemRefine consistently meets target budgets while preserving downstream performance and outperforming rule-based baselines under tight budgets.

We develop a novel multi-stage retrieval and reranking pipeline to construct the initial clause pair mapping, with a subset of clause pairs subsequently annotated by legal experts as Equivalent or Not Equivalent. The dataset comprises 14,727 clause pairs from 204 contracts across 8 agreement types, of which 3,000 are manually labelled: 900 train, 600 dev, and 1,500 test. We evaluate 12 models across 4 techniques, achieving a best macro-F1 of 65.11%, establishing LAUKIN as a challenging benchmark. Result: 成功发布了高质量的BioStance数据集，该数据集保留了分层对话语境，在生物伦理讨论中展现出高度的标注一致性，为生物伦理语境下的立场检测和论证挖掘研究提供了关键支持。

Conclusion: BioStance为生物伦理学领域的立场检测提供了重要的基准数据集，填补了大规模、特定领域社交媒体语境标注数据的空白，有助于提升计算模型对复杂争议性议题的分析能力。

Abstract: Bioethical debates increasingly unfold on social media, yet stance detection research lacks large-scale, domain-specific resources for modeling such context-dependent discourse. We present BioStance, a context-aware dataset of 39,600 annotated Post-Comment pairs from Reddit bioethical discussions. BioStance covers six controversial targets across three dimensions of bioethical controversy: fundamental value conflicts, individual liberty versus collective responsibility, and technological uncertainty. Each instance preserves hierarchical conversational context and is labeled by three independent annotators using a three-class stance scheme: Favor, Against, and None. The annotations achieve a mean Krippendorff's $α$ of 0.82, indicating substantial reliability. By combining thematic diversity, conversational structure, and high-quality human annotation, BioStance supports research on context-aware stance detection, argument mining, and computational analysis of bioethical discourse.

</details>


### [40] [SICI: A Semantic-Pragmatic Complexity Index Reveals Regime Shifts in LLM Stance Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13189)
*Fuqiang Niu,Bowen Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了立场推断复杂度指数（SICI），用于诊断LLM在立场检测任务中的性能瓶颈。研究发现，随着语义复杂度提升，LLM的错误模式呈现出一种类似物理相变的演变规律，现有的主流提示和增强技术难以突破这一认知边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管提示工程广泛应用，但LLM在立场检测任务中面对复杂样本时往往表现不佳，且常规改进方法（如指令优化、检索、辩论等）难以有效修复这些“硬样本”。因此，需要一种诊断指标来量化任务难度，并深入理解LLM在复杂场景下的失败机制。

Method: 1. 提出SICI（立场推断复杂度指数），包含七个维度，用于量化立场检测目标与文本对之间的语义-语用负荷。
2. 在SemEval-2016和VAST数据集上验证了SICI对LLM准确率的预测能力，并进行跨标注者一致性分析。
3. 通过对比GPT-3.5、GPT-4o等模型在不同SICI水平下的表现，分析错误模式的转移规律。
4. 进行15种干预方法（包括Prompting、检索增强、辩论等）的实证研究，探讨其对模型表现的影响。

Result: 1. SICI指标能够比表面特征更准确地预测LLM的准确率，且具有高度可靠性。
2. LLM的错误模式随SICI增加呈现“相变”特征：低复杂度样本倾向于过度归因（尤其是误判为Against），中等复杂度样本边界不稳定，高复杂度样本则迅速聚类为None（不相关/无法判断）。
3. 即使是目前最强的LLM（如GPT-4o），该错误模式依然存在，仅表现为复杂度边界的位移。
4. 现有的15种干预措施未能解决高复杂度样本带来的瓶颈，仅是在模型输出的归因与拒绝回答之间进行切换。

Conclusion: SICI指标有效揭示了立场检测中LLM的性能边界及其随复杂度变化的相变特征。现有的提示工程和检索增强方法大多只是在“过度归因”与“拒绝回答”之间权衡，而非真正提升模型处理复杂语义的能力。未来的研究应聚焦于如何通过模型架构改进或特定领域数据训练来突破这一性能瓶颈。

Abstract: Prompt-based LLMs are increasingly used for stance detection, but harder examples are not always repaired by clearer instructions, reasoning prompts, retrieval, or debate. We introduce SICI (Stance Inference Complexity Index), a seven-dimensional diagnostic measure of the semantic-pragmatic burden imposed by a target--text pair. Across SemEval-2016 and VAST, SICI predicts LLM accuracy better than surface proxies and shows substantial cross-scorer reliability ($α=0.771$). More importantly, LLM errors change regime as SICI increases: low-complexity examples invite over-attribution, especially Against predictions; intermediate examples form an unstable boundary; and high-complexity examples rapidly concentrate on None. This phase-transition-like structure persists across GPT-3.5, GPT-4o-mini, DeepSeek-V3, and GPT-4o, although stronger models move the boundaries. A 15-method intervention study further shows that prompting, retrieval, and debate often shift models along the attribution--abstention axis rather than removing the high-complexity bottleneck.
