Method: 提出了Agentified Agent Assessment (AAA) 评估范式，利用标准化协议A2A（任务管理）和MCP（工具访问）实现评估者与被评估者之间的统一交互；并开发了AgentBeats作为其具体实现，包含五种针对真实世界约束（如隐私、开放性）的评估模式。

Result: 通过五个月的开放竞赛（298个评判智能体与467个被测智能体）以及代码生成智能体的案例研究，证实了AAA框架在异构场景下具备高覆盖率、实用性和评估保真度，能够发掘传统方法难以捕捉的性能差异。

Conclusion: AAA框架和AgentBeats通过标准化的交互协议（A2A和MCP）成功统一了智能体评估标准，打破了现有评估体系碎片化和不兼容的壁垒，为智能体评估领域提供了一个可扩展、可复用且具备高保真度的通用评估范式。

Abstract: Agent systems are advancing quickly across domains, but their evaluation remains fragmented. Most benchmarks rely on fixed, LLM-centric harnesses that require heavy integration, create test-production mismatch, and limit fair comparison across diverse agent designs. The root problem is the lack of an open, agent-agnostic assessment interface. We advocate Agentified Agent Assessment (AAA), where evaluation is performed by judge agents and all participants interact through standardized protocols: A2A for task management and MCP for tool access. Conventional benchmarking defines two separate interfaces, one for the benchmark and one for the agent, while AAA only needs one; this yields a generic, unified framework that separates assessment logic from agent implementation and enables reproducible, interoperable, and multi-agent evaluation. We further introduce AgentBeats as a concrete realization of AAA: we identify five practical operation modes that make standardized assessment compatible with real-world constraints on openness, privacy, and reproducibility.
  To evaluate our design at scale, we conduct two studies: a five-month open competition that drew 298 judge agents across 12 categories together with 467 subject agents from independent participants, showing that AAA applies across a heterogeneous range of benchmarks; and a case study on coding agents that confirms agentified evaluation preserves fidelity with the public record while surfacing previously missing head-to-head results, yielding research insights about agent design. Combining a community-scale field study and a controlled coding case study, we verify that AAA delivers coverage, practicality, and fidelity across heterogeneous scenarios at scale. Together, AAA and AgentBeats offer a clear path toward open, standardized, and reproducible agent assessment.

### [156] [Beyond Runtime Enforcement: Shield Synthesis as Defensibility Analysis for Adversarial Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13621)
*Achraf Hsain,Sultan Almuhammadi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出将屏蔽式强化学习从“运行时安全约束工具”转型为“设计时系统架构分析工具”，通过构建对抗博弈与“防御指纹”，量化并评估网络架构的可防御性，从而辅助安全决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点将屏蔽式强化学习仅视为一种运行时的安全约束机制，作者认为这种定位存在偏差。该研究旨在论证这些自动机理论工具在设计阶段更具价值，可用于提供关于系统架构安全性的结构性洞察，而非仅仅限制代理（agent）的运行时行为。

Method: 1. 将自动机理论（规范编译、乘积博弈构建、吸引子计算、获胜区域提取）重新定义为设计时的分析框架；2. 构建受限的两人安全博弈模型进行网络防御分析，对攻击者和防御者的规范进行不对称约束；3. 推导拓扑层面的防御指标，结合受屏蔽约束的对抗性多智能体强化学习（MARL）后收敛行为；4. 生成“防御指纹”（Defensibility Fingerprint），并进行“假设分析”（What-if analysis）以对比形式化安全与操作有效性。

Result: 该方法能够产生形式化的“防御判定”（defensibility verdict），即证明特定拓扑结构在给定规范下是否可防御的证书。实验表明，形式化的防御界限与系统的实际操作表现（operational effectiveness）存在差异，小的架构调整可能显著改变操作结果，但对形式化安全边际影响微小，验证了该框架在回答架构安全问题上的效用。

Conclusion: 屏蔽式强化学习（Shielded RL）在安全领域的真正价值不应局限于运行时的策略限制，而应定位为设计阶段的分析工具。通过形式化方法评估系统的“防御指纹”，能够为网络架构决策提供关键的安全性洞察，区分形式化安全界限与实际运行表现。

Abstract: Shielded reinforcement learning is typically presented as a runtime safety mechanism that compiles temporal-logic specifications into automata restricting an agent's actions. We argue this is the wrong product. The same automata-theoretic machinery -- specification compilation, product game construction, attractor computation, and winning-region extraction -- is better read as a design-time analytical instrument whose outputs are structural insights about a system rather than runtime constraints on a deployed agent.
  We instantiate this through a constrained two-player safety game for network defense. The two specifications are enforced asymmetrically: the defender specification defines the unsafe region of the game, whereas the attacker specification restricts the adversary's legal actions during attractor computation. Solving the game yields a defensibility verdict -- a formal certificate that a topology-specification pair is or is not defensible -- with the associated winning region and shield.
  Beyond the binary verdict, we derive topology-level metrics from the attractor structure and combine them with post-convergence behavior from shield-constrained adversarial multi-agent reinforcement learning. Together these form a defensibility fingerprint capturing both a network's formal safety properties and its operational behavior under adaptive play.
  A what-if analysis shows that formal defensibility and operational effectiveness capture distinct aspects of security: small architectural changes can produce large shifts in operational outcomes while leaving formal safety margins nearly unchanged. Shield synthesis is thus most valuable not as a deployment mechanism for safe agents, but as a framework for answering architectural questions about whether, where, and how a system can be defended. The defensibility verdict is the output, not the safe policy.

</details>


### [157] [Before You Think: System 0, AI-Mediated Cognition and Cognitive Colonization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13658)
*Marianna Bergamaschi Ganapini,Massimo Chiriatti,Enrico Panai,Giuseppe Riva*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探讨了AI对人类认知的深层影响，对比了三种主要认知框架，提出了“认知殖民”概念，揭示了AI如何通过隐蔽方式嵌入用户思维结构并施加影响，强调了识别此类隐形干预的必要性与紧迫性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨人工智能对人类认知和知识论的深远影响。作者关注现有的理论框架是否足以涵盖AI对人类思维过程的潜在干预，特别是AI如何通过隐蔽方式将外部利益嵌入用户的认知架构之中。

Method: 对比分析法。文章通过对“三系统理论（Tri-System Theory）”、“思维框架（Thinkframes）”和“系统0（System 0）”三种框架的哲学考察，分析它们在解释AI对个体推理和集体认知实践影响方面的异同，并引入“认知殖民”这一核心概念进行理论阐释。

Result: 研究表明，“三系统理论”和“思维框架”虽有其价值，但均无法完全覆盖“系统0”所指涉的独特性。作者指出，“认知殖民”现象使得AI能够在用户难以察觉的情况下，深度嵌入并引导个体的思维与决策过程。

Conclusion: “系统0”概念揭示了AI对人类认知深刻且隐蔽的重塑作用。作者强调，理解“认知殖民”现象对于应对当前广泛部署的AI系统至关重要，这不仅是一个理论课题，更是紧迫的实践任务。

Abstract: This paper examines three recent frameworks for understanding the cognitive and epistemic consequences of artificial intelligence: Tri-System Theory, Thinkframes, and System 0. It argues that while the first two capture important dimensions of AI's influence on individual reasoning and collective epistemic practices, System 0 occupies a theoretically distinctive position that neither can fully replicate. The paper introduces the concept of cognitive colonization, according to which AI systems can embed external interests within the architecture of the self in ways that are difficult for users to perceive. Because such systems are already widely deployed, understanding these invisible forms of influence is an urgent philosophical and practical task.

</details>


### [158] [EurekAgent: Agent Environment Engineering is All You Need For Autonomous Scientific Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13662)
*Amy Xin,Jiening Siow,Junjie Wang,Zijun Yao,Fanjin Zhang,Jian Song,Lei Hou,Juanzi Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了“环境工程”框架，通过构建优化后的运行环境，使 EurekAgent 在低成本下实现了高效、自主的科学发现并刷新了多项任务的最佳性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型能力的提升，自主科研的瓶颈已从“设计智能体工作流”转向“构建智能体环境”，需要通过环境工程来放大探索效率并抑制奖励欺诈等负面行为。

Method: 提出了名为 EurekAgent 的环境工程化智能体系统，该系统从四个维度对环境进行优化：权限工程（限制执行与隔离评估）、制品工程（通过文件系统与 Git 进行协作）、预算工程（预算感知探索）以及人机协同工程（简化监督与干预）。

Result: EurekAgent 在数学、内核工程和机器学习等多个任务中刷新了最优性能，特别是以不到 11 美元的 API 成本发现了 26 圆填充问题的最新最优解。

Conclusion: 环境工程（Environment Engineering）是推动自主科学发现的关键，通过系统化设计智能体运行的资源、约束和交互界面，能够有效提升智能体的科研效率与安全性。

Abstract: LLM-based agents have shown increasing potential in automating scientific discovery. Given an optimizable metric and an execution environment, they can propose, validate, and iterate scientific solutions, and have produced results that outperform human-designed approaches. As model capabilities continue to improve, we argue that the bottleneck for autonomous scientific discovery is shifting from prescribing agent workflows to designing agent environments: the resources, constraints, and interfaces that shape agent behavior. We frame this as environment engineering: building environments that amplify productive behaviors, such as open-ended exploration, systematic artifact management, and inter-agent collaboration, while suppressing harmful behaviors, such as reward hacking and high-friction human oversight. We present EurekAgent, an environment-engineered agent system for metric-driven autonomous scientific discovery. EurekAgent engineers the environment along four dimensions: permissions engineering for bounded agent execution and isolated evaluation; artifact engineering for filesystem and Git-based collaboration; budget engineering for budget-aware exploration; and human-in-the-loop engineering for easy human supervision and intervention. EurekAgent sets new state-of-the-art results on multiple mathematics, kernel engineering, and machine learning tasks, including new state-of-the-art 26-circle packing results discovered with less than $11 in total API cost. We open-source our code and results, and call for environment engineering as a core research direction for developing reliable autonomous research agents.

### [159] [Agents-K1: Towards Agent-native Knowledge Orchestration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13669)
*Zongsheng Cao,Bihao Zhan,Jinxin Shi,Jiong Wang,Fangchen Yu,Zhijie Zhong,Zijie Guo,Tianshuo Peng,Zhuo Liu,Yi Xie,Xiang Zhuang,Yue Fan,Runmin Ma,Shiyang Feng,Xiangchao Yan,Anran Liu,Peng Ye,Wenlong Zhang,Shufei Zhang,Chunfeng Song,Fenghua Ling,Jie Zhou,Liang He,Bo Zhang,Lei Bai*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于大模型的科研智能体大多仅关注流程编排，忽略了对科学知识的深度组织。现有方法通常只处理摘要或简单的引用关系，缺乏对论文中关键实体、声明、证据和方法论血缘等核心要素的提取，限制了智能体进行深层次科学推理的能力。

Method: 提出了 Agents-K1 流水线：1. 多模态解析器，能够提取全篇论文中的实体、证据、引用及关系；2. 基于 GRPO 训练的 4B 信息抽取骨干模型；3. graphanything CLI，支持网页搜索、图检索及跨文档遍历的统一智能体接口。此外，利用该流水线构建了包含 246 万篇论文的大规模知识图谱 Scholar-KG。

Result: 实验表明，Agents-K1 在科学信息抽取、知识图谱构建以及多跳科学推理任务中均表现出优越的性能，并成功发布了包含 100 万篇论文的子集 Scholar-KG 供科研使用。

Conclusion: Agents-K1 成功将非结构化的科学文献转化为结构化的知识图谱，通过构建 Scholar-KG 弥补了现有智能体在深度科学推理上的知识获取短板，为科学研究智能体提供了一个更强大的底层知识基础设施。

Abstract: Current LLM-based research agents have advanced through agent orchestration, yet largely overlook scientific knowledge orchestration. Existing works often reduce papers to abstracts, surface mentions, and flat \texttt{cites} edges, omitting key entities, claims, evidence, mechanisms, and method lineages essential for scientific reasoning. To this end, we introduce \textbf{Agents-K1}, an end-to-end knowledge orchestration pipeline that converts raw documents into agent-native scientific knowledge graphs. Agents-K1 integrates three components under a unifying theoretical foundation: a multimodal parser whose five-module schema captures entities, multimodal evidence, citations, and typed inter-entity relations across the full paper rather than abstracts alone; a 4B information-extraction backbone trained with GRPO under a rule-based reward; and a graphanything CLI, a tri-source agent interface that unifies web search, multimodal graph retrieval, and cross-document traversal. On top of this, we process 2.46 million scientific papers across six subjects to produce \textbf{Scholar-KG}, of which we release a one-million-paper subset, and the full Scholar-KG is accessible via the SCP link below. The same pipeline can be extended to general-domain corpora and to schema-conformant data synthesis. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Agents-K1 achieves superior performance in scientific information extraction, knowledge graph construction, and multi-hop scientific reasoning.

### [160] [Automated reproducibility assessments in the social and behavioral sciences using large language models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13670)
*Tobias Holtdirk,Pietro Marcolongo,Anna Steinberg Schulten,Felix Henninger,Stefan Rose,Sarah Ball,Bolei Ma,Frauke Kreuter,Markus Weinmann,Stefan Feuerriegel*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究展示了大语言模型能够自动化评估社会与行为科学研究的可重复性，在效应量恢复和结论一致性方面表现优于人类再分析者，提供了一种高效、可扩展的审计工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社会与行为科学中的可重复性评估目前主要依赖独立研究者进行人工重新分析，这种方法资源消耗巨大且难以扩展。因此，研究者寻求开发一种基于大语言模型的自动化、高效的评估方法。

Method: 研究人员构建了一个自动化管道，利用大语言模型（LLMs）对76项社会与行为科学领域的已发表研究进行再分析。通过对比LLM生成的分析结果与原始研究结论及人类独立再分析结果，评估其可重复性。在评估指标上，采用Cohen's d（±0.05误差范围）来衡量效应量恢复情况，并比较结论的一致性。

Result: 在76项研究中，LLM在排除7项无法产生有效效应量估计的研究后，41%的研究恢复了原始效应量，96%的研究在定性结论上与原始研究一致。相比之下，人类再分析者仅恢复了34%的原始效应量，并在74%的情况下得出相同定性结论。

Conclusion: 大语言模型（LLMs）证明了其作为一种可扩展、自动化工具在社会与行为科学领域进行可重复性评估的潜力，为系统性审计实证结果奠定了基础。

Abstract: Reproducibility in the social and behavioral sciences is typically evaluated by independent researchers who reanalyze the original data to assess whether the published findings can be recovered. However, such approaches are resource-intensive and difficult to scale. Here, we show that large language models (LLMs) can automate reproducibility assessments. Using N=76 published studies with predefined claims from the behavioral and social sciences, we compare LLM-generated analysis with the original findings and human reanalysis. For 7 studies, the LLM could not produce a viable effect size estimate. For the remaining studies, our LLM pipeline recovered the original effect sizes in 41% of studies using a +/-0.05 tolerance in Cohen's d. Further, our LLM pipeline reached the same qualitative conclusion as the original study in 96% of cases, where conclusions indicate whether the reanalysis supports the original claim. For comparison, human reanalysts recovered the original effect sizes in 34% of studies and reached the same qualitative conclusion in 74% of cases. Together, these results show that LLMs can serve as a scalable tool for automated reproducibility assessment and provide a foundation for systematic auditing of empirical results in the social and behavioral sciences.

### [161] [Quickest Detection of Hallucination Onset: Delay Bounds and Learned CUSUM Statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12476)
*Igor Itkin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出从“最快变点检测”的角度评估大模型幻觉，指出传统的分类指标掩盖了关键的实时延迟问题，并通过序列分析揭示了检测器在信息论层面的性能局限与优化路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的幻觉检测评估主要依赖分类指标（AUC），忽视了流式应用中至关重要的“检测延迟”指标。研究旨在揭示幻觉检测中的实时监测性能及其背后的理论极限。

Method: 将幻觉检测建模为“最快变点检测”（Quickest Change Detection）问题；利用一阶马尔可夫模型导出Lorden下界；提出一种基于因果循环标记器（Causal Recurrent Labeler）的方法，将其等效为CUSUM算法；引入Donsker-Varadhan型信息率最优定理来分析性能差距。

Result: 在RAGTruth数据集上，该方法在保持相同误报率的情况下，将检测延迟从线性基线的31个Token降低至11-13个Token；理论分析显示，目前的学习模型仅能获取特征中约1/4.5的散度信息，存在显著的性能提升空间。

Conclusion: 现有的分类指标无法衡量幻觉检测的实时性能。通过将幻觉检测建模为序列分析问题，研究表明当前的检测器距离信息论极限仍有显著差距，且该差距主要归因于单步得分的准确性，而非简单的累积机制。

Abstract: Token-level hallucination detectors are evaluated as classifiers, by AUC over all tokens, yet a streaming monitor is judged by its reaction time: the number of tokens that pass between the onset of a hallucination and the alarm. We formulate hallucination onset detection as a quickest change detection problem. A first-order Markov model of the latent faithful/hallucinated state, validated on RAGTruth, places the task inside classical change-point theory and yields Lorden's lower bound on detection delay: about 1.3 tokens at a false-alarm rate of 0.01. We then show that a causal recurrent labeler acts as a CUSUM with a learned increment; at a matched false-alarm rate it detects in 11-13 tokens, against 31 for a linear per-token baseline, and a controlled decomposition attributes most of this advantage to a better per-token score rather than to temporal accumulation. An information-rate optimality theorem of Donsker-Varadhan type explains the remaining order-of-magnitude gap: the learned score realizes only 1/4.5 of the divergence the features carry, a deficit that recalibration cannot remove, with the remainder a finite-horizon effect. Classification metrics conceal this delay structure; sequential analysis makes it measurable

</details>


### [162] [Boltzmann Attention: Learnable Ising Couplings for Cooperative Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12478)
*Gilhan Kim,Daniel K. Park*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种“玻尔兹曼注意力”机制，通过引入Ising模型及其可学习的成对耦合，显式捕捉位置间的复杂交互，显著提升了长序列建模能力，并展示了其在量子退火训练下的应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的Softmax注意力机制主要通过独立的查询-键相似度计算相关性，缺乏对注意力决策之间交互关系的显式参数化建模，从而限制了模型处理位置间复杂协同或拮抗结构的能力。

Method: 提出了一种基于能量的“玻尔兹曼注意力”（Boltzmann attention）机制。该方法使用Ising模型来建模注意力模式，通过在传统的局部场（query-key相关性）基础上引入可学习的成对耦合（pairwise couplings），使得模型能够显式地捕捉位置之间的合作或拮抗关系，并利用绝热量子退火作为一种可行的训练策略。

Result: 在字符级语言建模和合成括号匹配任务中的实验表明，玻尔兹曼注意力在标准Transformer架构下始终优于传统的Softmax注意力，且随序列长度增加优势更加显著；消融实验证实了性能提升主要源于可学习的成对耦合；同时验证了绝热量子退火在实际训练中的可行性。

Conclusion: 明确的位置间相互作用为基于注意力机制的序列建模提供了一种原则性的改进路径。Ising模型框架不仅增强了注意力机制的建模能力，还为利用量子计算（如绝热量子退火）进行高效训练提供了理论与实践基础。

Abstract: Attention mechanisms are central to modern sequence models, yet standard attention computes relevance primarily through individual query--key similarities. Although softmax normalization introduces competition among positions, a standard attention layer does not explicitly parameterize learnable interactions between attention decisions. This limits its ability to directly model cooperative or antagonistic co-attention structure within the attention mechanism itself. We propose Boltzmann attention, an energy-based generalization in which attention patterns are governed by an interacting Ising model. The method augments the usual data-dependent local fields with learnable pairwise couplings, allowing the model to represent inter-position correlations beyond those captured by softmax or sigmoid attention. Experiments on character-level language modeling and synthetic bracket matching show that Boltzmann attention consistently improves over standard softmax attention within a standard Transformer architecture, with the advantage becoming more pronounced as sequence length increases. A four-way ablation confirms that the improvement arises from the learnable pairwise couplings. These results suggest that explicit inter-position interactions provide a principled enhancement for attention-based sequence modeling. Moreover, the Ising formulation opens a natural path toward quantum-computing-based sampling strategies: we demonstrate that diabatic quantum annealing provides a practical training method while maintaining competitive performance with exact Boltzmann computation.

</details>


### [163] [ReCal: Reward Calibration for RL-based LLM Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12479)
*Qihang Yu,Hanwen Tong,Zhengqi Zhang,Bo Zheng,Feng Wei,Shengyu Zhang,Zemin Liu,Fei Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对强化学习大模型路由中奖励信号单一、模糊及样本间差异导致的优化偏差问题，提出了 ReCal 框架，通过分层奖励分解和分布感知校准，显著提升了路由系统的训练效果与稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于强化学习的 LLM 路由方法在处理异构任务时，因将多个优化目标（如正确性、格式规范）合并为单一标量奖励，导致信用分配模糊；同时，不同任务间奖励信号差异巨大，导致模型倾向于优化简单样本，影响模型性能和训练稳定性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ReCal 的奖励校准框架：1. 引入分层奖励分解机制，实现组件级的优势估计，解决多目标奖励聚合导致的模糊信用分配问题；2. 采用分布感知优化策略，通过方差感知重加权和数据集内归一化，平衡不同任务和样本间的奖励差异，减轻优化偏差。

Result: 在七个数据集上的实验结果表明，ReCal 方法在性能和训练稳定性方面均显著优于现有基线方法，能够更有效地发挥大模型路由的协同优势。

Conclusion: ReCal 通过分层奖励分解和分布感知优化策略，有效解决了强化学习路由中奖励信号模糊和优化偏差的问题，为提升大语言模型路由系统的性能和稳定性提供了一种鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) routing has emerged as an effective paradigm for leveraging the complementary strengths of multiple LLMs through dynamic model and reasoning-strategy selection. Recent reinforcement learning (RL)-based routing methods further improve routing quality by optimizing routing policies from interaction feedback. However, they still struggle to provide informative and comparable learning signals under heterogeneous tasks with varying difficulty. In practice, multiple objectives (e.g., correctness, format behavior) are aggregated into a single scalar reward, leading to ambiguous credit assignment and conflicting optimization signals. Moreover, reward signals exhibit significant variability across instances, where some instances produce higher or more variable rewards, introducing optimization bias that favors trivial samples over informative ones. To address these issues, we propose \textbf{ReCal}, a \textbf{\underline{Re}}ward \textbf{\underline{Cal}}ibration framework for RL-based LLM routing. We first introduce a hierarchical reward decomposition mechanism with component-wise advantage estimation. We further propose a distribution-aware optimization strategy that calibrates optimization variability through variance-aware reweighting and per-dataset normalization. Experiments on seven datasets demonstrate that ReCal consistently improves routing performance, and training stability over baselines. Code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/ReCal.

</details>


### [164] [Representing Time Series as Structured Programs for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12481)
*Jaeho Kim,Changhun Oh,Seokhyun Lee,Irina Rish,Changhee Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需训练的 T2SP 方法，通过将时间序列转化为符号化程序，消除了大模型处理时间序列时的模态差异，显著提升了模型在时间序列理解与推理任务上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多采用原始数值序列输入或对模型进行微调，这会给大模型带来沉重的特征提取负担，并引发模态不匹配问题，导致长序列处理性能下降且计算开销巨大。因此，需要一种更高效的方式将时间序列信息呈现给大模型。

Method: 提出了 T2SP（Time-Series-to-Structured-Program）方法，这是一种无需训练的确定性算法。该方法将原始时间序列分解为趋势、周期和显著事件，并将其转换为一种结构化的符号程序格式，使其更符合大模型处理代码和文本的逻辑。

Result: 在编辑、描述和问答三类推理任务中，T2SP 表现优于原始字符串表示法，具体表现为：模型推理性能显著提升、推理时间缩短、任务失败率降低。

Conclusion: T2SP 提供了一种有效的接口，能够将时间序列数据转化为大模型易于理解的结构化程序，证明了通过优化数据表示方法，无需额外训练即可提升大模型在时间序列任务上的性能。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong reasoning and instruction-following capabilities, making them potentially powerful tools for time-series analysis. However, time series lie outside their native textual modality, raising a fundamental question: how should time series be represented so that LLMs can reason about them effectively? Existing work typically serializes raw numerical sequences or fine-tunes pre-trained LLMs on time-series data. These approaches place the burden of extracting temporal structure directly on the LLM, creating a modality mismatch that often degrades performance on long sequences and introduces substantial computational overhead. In this work, we introduce Time-Series-to-Structured-Program representation (T2SP), a deterministic, training-free method that represents a time series as a structured symbolic program. T2SP decomposes time series into trends, periods, and salient events, expressing them in a program-friendly format aligned with the textual and code-like modalities on which LLMs are natively trained. By shifting temporal-structure extraction from the model to the representation itself, T2SP enables off-the-shelf LLMs to leverage their existing reasoning capabilities for time-series understanding. We evaluate T2SP on three reasoning tasks -- editing, captioning, and question answering -- where it consistently improves performance, reduces reasoning time, and lowers failure rates compared with raw-string representations. Our results demonstrate that T2SP provides an effective interface between time series and LLMs.

### [165] [Scalable anomaly detection via a univariate Christoffel function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12483)
*Florian Grivet,Didier Henrion,Jean-Bernard Lasserre,Louise Travé-Massuyès*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对传统克里斯托费尔函数方法在高维数据中计算不可行的缺陷，本文提出了 UCF 方法，通过将计算转化为基于距离的一元函数，有效解决了维度灾难，并在多项基准测试中展现了领先的异常检测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的基于克里斯托费尔函数（Christoffel Function）的异常检测方法虽然具有坚实的数学基础，但受限于计算复杂度——其核心步骤涉及维度指数级增长的矩阵求逆，导致其无法处理中高维度数据集，限制了实际应用。

Method: 提出了一种名为 UCF（Univariate Christoffel Function）的新方法。该方法不再直接对多维数据进行复杂的矩阵求逆，而是基于查询点与支撑点之间的平方距离，构造一元克里斯托费尔函数，从而规避了维度指数级增长带来的计算瓶颈。

Result: 在 ADBench 基准测试中，UCF 方法在平均精度（Average Precision）指标上表现优异，持续超越了 14 种先进的基准算法。

Conclusion: UCF 方法通过简化计算复杂度，不仅保留了克里斯托费尔函数在异常检测中的理论优势，还显著提升了算法的可扩展性，使其成为一种高效、稳健且具有广泛适用性的异常检测工具。

Abstract: Anomaly detection plays a critical role in identifying unusual patterns across domains such as fraud detection, network intrusion, and system fault diagnosis. Recently, Christoffel function-based methods, rooted in polynomial optimization, have emerged as promising alternatives to deep learning due to their strong mathematical foundations and computational frugality. However, their practical applicability is hindered by the need to invert a matrix whose size grows exponentially with the data dimension, rendering the method intractable even for moderate-dimensional datasets. This paper addresses the dimensionality limitations of Christoffel function-based anomaly detection while preserving its key theoretical properties, i.e., the on-off support dichotomy behavior and the accurate support shape capture. We introduce UCF, a univariate Christoffel function which is based on the squared distance between the query point and the support points. Extensive experiments on the ADBench benchmark demonstrate that UCF consistently outperforms 14 state-of-the-art baselines in terms of Average Precision. By resolving the scalability bottleneck of the Christoffel Function, this work expands the toolkit of anomaly detection methods with a robust, theoretically grounded, and universally applicable approach.

### [166] [Speculative Rollback Correction for Quality-Diverse Web Agent Imitation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12485)
*Longkun Hao,Hongyu Lin,Hao Li,Zhichao Yang,Haojie Hao,Dongshuo Huang,Haitao Yang,Hongyu Ge,Ming jie Xie,Yanjun Wu,Zi Hao Yin,Yan Bai,Yihang Lou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为 SRC 的 Web 智能体训练框架，通过短时投机执行与按需专家干预（而非全程干预），解决了模仿学习中专家依赖与误差累积的矛盾，显著提升了智能体的训练质量与轨迹多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在利用专家轨迹训练交互式 Web 智能体时，确定专家干预的适当时机是关键挑战。干预过晚会导致误差累积使状态不可逆，而干预过早或过多则会产生“专家依赖”，导致智能体缺乏自主性，陷入单一轨迹的局部最优。因此，需要一种更高效的干预策略。

Method: 提出了一种名为“投机回滚纠错”（Speculative Rollback Correction, SRC）的分支级模仿学习框架。其核心思想是采用固定视角的“分支回顾”机制：学生智能体执行一段短促的投机性轨迹，仅在局部进度失效时才触发教师纠错。此外，通过回滚机制保留有效的状态前缀，并利用硬验证器过滤出成功的轨迹存储在质量多样性库中，从而增强下一步动作的监督微调。

Result: 在 WebArena-Infinity 基准测试中，SRC 成功收集了 977 条通过验证的轨迹和 9,183 个下一步动作示例。实验结果表明，固定视角的回顾机制在恢复能力与查询成本之间实现了比步骤级回顾更好的权衡，同时保留了多种通过验证的解决方案。

Conclusion: SRC 通过引入分支级模仿学习框架，有效地平衡了专家干预的频率与模型自主性，解决了以往交互式 Web 智能体在模仿学习中面临的依赖专家策略导致训练陷入局部最优，或干预延迟导致状态不可逆的问题。该方法在 WebArena-Infinity 基准测试中展现了卓越的性能。

Abstract: Training interactive web agents through imitation learning from expert trajectories has emerged as a highly effective approach. However, determining the optimal timing for expert intervention presents a critical challenge in this context. Delayed intervention often leads to the accumulation of early-stage errors, pushing the page state into an irrecoverable regime. Conversely, premature or excessive intervention causes the agent to become overly reliant on expert policies, trapping the model in local optima characterized by a single, rigid trajectory. We propose Speculative Rollback Correction (SRC), a branch-level imitation framework for resettable agent environments. Instead of requesting teacher labels at every visited state or correcting only after a completed trajectory, SRC uses fixed-horizon branch review: the student executes a short speculative segment before teacher review, and the teacher localizes the first harmful deviation only when local progress breaks. Rollback preserves useful prefixes, while successful rollouts are filtered by a hard verifier and retained in a lightweight quality-diversity archive. The resulting data supports next-action supervised fine-tuning on both localized corrections and verifier-passing trajectories. On WebArena-Infinity, SRC collects 977 verifier-passing trajectories and 9,183 next-action examples; fixed-horizon review improves the recovery-versus-query tradeoff over step-level review while retaining verifier-passing solution variants. Code is available at https://github.com/LongkunHao/SRC_gui_agent.

Abstract: Condition-based Predictive Maintenance (PdM) for truck fleets has gained momentum in recent years. It involves selecting only the most recent observations from the time series and transforming them into a tabular format for classification using machine learning (ML) models designed for tabular data. ### [168] [DynamicPTQ: Mitigating Activation Quantization Collapse via Residual-Stream Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12487)
*Zimo Zhao,Maolin Wang,Bowen Yu,Bowen Liu,Xiao Han,Xiangyu Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对4-bit大模型推理中极端激活值导致的精度损失问题，本文提出DynamicPTQ，通过分析残差流动态特性，对敏感层实施动态混合精度量化，在保障精度的同时有效提升了推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在将权重、激活值及KV缓存同时量化为4-bit时，极端激活值（massive activations）会导致严重的量化误差。现有基于平滑变换的方法忽略了残差流的跨层动态特性，难以处理随网络深度周期性出现和消失的异常值，导致量化后的模型性能显著下降。

Method: 提出了一种动态后训练量化策略（DynamicPTQ）。首先通过定义“跳跃比（Jump Ratio）”和“历史特征信噪比（Historical Feature SNR）”量化分析残差流的动态特性；随后根据残差流的阶段性演变规律，识别出对量化敏感的层，仅在这些层使用8-bit激活量化，而其余层保持4-bit，从而实现阶段感知的混合精度量化。该方法可与QuaRot、SpinQuant等现有PTQ技术兼容。

Result: 在LLaMA-2和LLaMA-3模型上的实验表明，DynamicPTQ在W4A4KV4量化配置下显著降低了困惑度（perplexity），提升了零样本问答（zero-shot QA）性能，并在适度增加内存开销的前提下，将推理吞吐量提升了1.05至1.07倍。

Conclusion: 本文提出的DynamicPTQ通过捕捉大模型层间残差流的动态特性，有效解决了全4-bit量化中的极端激活值问题，证明了基于层级敏感度的混合精度策略在保持模型推理性能与提升吞吐量方面的实用价值，为低比特大模型推理提供了一种鲁棒的优化方案。

Abstract: Post-training quantization (PTQ) is essential for efficient large language model inference, but reliably quantizing activations remains challenging when weights, activations, and KV caches are all quantized to 4-bit precision. A key difficulty lies in massive activations, whose extreme values dominate the activation range and amplify quantization errors. State-of-the-art methods mainly mitigate massive activations through transformation-based smoothing, such as orthogonal rotations and affine scaling, but overlook the cross-layer dynamics of the residual stream. In this paper, we show that massive activations emerge and disappear in a phase-wise pattern across network depth, triggering large residual changes. These changes cause newly injected layer-wise updates to dominate the 4-bit quantization scale and weaken historical residual information. To characterize this behavior, we introduce Jump Ratio and Historical Feature SNR. This suggests that static transformation-based smoothing cannot fully resolve dynamic quantization instability caused by cross-layer residual changes. Based on this analysis, we propose DynamicPTQ, a Dynamic Post-Training Quantization policy for phase-aware mixed-precision activation quantization. DynamicPTQ identifies quantization-sensitive layers from residual-stream dynamics and assigns 8-bit activation precision only to these layers, while keeping weights, KV caches, and other activations in 4-bit precision. It can be directly integrated with strong PTQ baselines such as QuaRot, SpinQuant, and FlatQuant. Experiments on LLaMA-2 and LLaMA-3 show that DynamicPTQ consistently improves perplexity and zero-shot QA performance under W4A4KV4 quantization, while achieving 1.05 to 1.07 times throughput improvement with modest memory overhead. These results demonstrate a practical path toward robust low-bit LLM inference.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在模型迭代更新过程中，如何保持特征表示的兼容性以避免大规模重新计算图像特征（即保证检索系统的连续性）是一个挑战。现有的简单分类器学习方法往往忽略了特征的高阶依赖关系。

Method: 提出利用d-Simplex固定分类器进行模型训练，并结合交叉熵损失与对比损失的凸组合，以捕捉特征分布中的高阶依赖关系，实现模型更新时的表示兼容性。

Result: 理论上证明了d-Simplex固定分类器学习的平稳表示满足兼容性定义；实验结果表明，该方法在顺序微调和模型替换场景下表现优异，在保持检索系统不中断的同时，显著提升了模型性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出通过结合d-Simplex固定分类器与对比损失函数，在模型更新和替换过程中实现特征表示的“平稳性”，从而保证了检索服务的连续性，无需重新处理数据库图像，并达到了最先进的性能。

Abstract: Learning compatible representations aims to learn feature representations that can be used interchangeably over time whenever a model undergoes updates. In this paper, we demonstrate that stationary representations learned by d-Simplex fixed classifiers imply compatibility as in its formal definition. This result establishes a foundation for future works and can be directly exploited in practical learning scenarios. We address the challenge of learning compatibility using $d$-Simplex fixed classifiers when the model is sequentially fine-tuned. Learning according to a d-Simplex fixed classifier with the cross-entropy loss aligns feature distributions at the first-order statistics. Consequently, it may not fully capture higher-order dependencies in the representation between model updates. To address this issue, we demonstrate that training the model using a $d$-Simplex fixed classifier through a convex combination of the cross-entropy loss and a contrastive loss not only captures higher-order dependencies, but is also equivalent to learning with the cross-entropy under the compatibility constraints. We confirm our findings with extensive experiments also considering a new scenario where a pre-trained model is sequentially fine-tuned and occasionally replaced with an improved model. We show that stationary representations enable uninterrupted retrieval services (without reprocessing gallery images) while improving performance during model updates and replacements, achieving state-of-the-art. Code at https://github.com/miccunifi/iamcl2r.

### [170] [Robustness Verification of Recurrent Neural Networks with Abstraction Refinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12490)
*Li-Jen Lin,Chih-Duo Hong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对RNN鲁棒性验证中非线性误差随时间累积的问题，本文提出了一种基于SHAP的时间步长细化框架，通过精确化关键时间步的激活函数来提高鲁棒性证明的紧致性与成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的循环神经网络（RNN）局部鲁棒性验证方法在处理长序列时，因非线性松弛带来的误差会随时间递归传播并不断累积，导致线性边界传播方法过于保守，难以证明输入样本的真实鲁棒性。

Method: 1. 抽象细化框架：通过对跨越零点的激活函数预激活区间进行划分，使ReLU函数在划分区间内变得精确，并显著收紧tanh和sigmoid函数的线性包络。
2. SHAP引导的策略：利用SHAP值评估各时间步对验证目标的贡献，仅对关键的时间步进行细化，从而在保持精度的同时控制了长序列验证的组合爆炸成本。

Result: 在CIFAR10和MNIST数据集上的实验表明，该方法在验证成功率和鲁棒性边界的紧致性方面优于单纯的抽象方法，并展示了在ReLU与tanh激活模型之间明确的运行时间权衡。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于SHAP引导的时间步长选择的抽象细化框架，有效解决了循环神经网络（RNN）验证中因非线性松弛误差随时间累积而导致的过度保守问题，为RNN的局部鲁棒性验证提供了更精确且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Certified local robustness verification for recurrent neural networks (RNNs) is challenging because approximation errors introduced by nonlinear relaxations can propagate through recurrent connections and accumulate over time. As a result, scalable linear bound propagation methods often become overly conservative and fail to certify inputs that are in fact robust, especially when many pre-activation intervals cross zero. We propose an abstraction-refinement framework for RNN verification that partitions such intervals to remove the dominant relaxation error: on each refined branch, ReLU becomes exact, and smooth activations such as tanh and sigmoid admit substantially tighter linear envelopes. To control the combinatorial cost of splitting in long sequences, we introduce a SHAP-guided timestep selection strategy that ranks hidden states by their contribution to the verification objective and refines only the most critical timesteps in temporal order. Experiments on CIFAR10 and MNIST stroke benchmarks demonstrate consistent improvements in verification success and robustness-margin tightness over abstraction-only baselines, while exposing clear runtime trade-offs between ReLU and tanh models.

### [171] [Net-Ev$^2$: A Generative Simulator for Network Event Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12494)

An even more challenging yet meaningful task is simulating how disturbance events (e.g., accidents) propagate their impacts across real-world networks. The existing approaches fall short of modeling both structured attributes and unstructured semantics of events, and capturing topological structures in simulating network event evolution. Therefore, we are motivated to propose Net-Ev$^2$ ($\underline{\textbf{Net}}$work $\underline{\textbf{Ev}}$ent $\underline{\textbf{Ev}}$olution), a novel generative simulator that jointly leverages event cues while preserving network topology in simulations. Specifically, the framework consists of two stages, namely structure-guided masked pre-training and topology-aware diffusion process, which is achieved by U-Net-like graph downsampling and upsampling during denoising. At inference time, Net-Ev$^2$ can generate simulations using natural-language event input only, with greater flexibility for practical usage. Furthermore, we introduce Net-Ev$^2$-6.5M, a multimodal benchmark of aligned event and network traffic data across four large-scale road networks, as well as a new topology-aware metric, namely JL-MMD, to evaluate topological fidelity in generated network dynamics. Extensive experiments demonstrate the state-of-the-art performance and strong generalization ability of Net-Ev$^2$. Code is made available at https://github.com/Guangyu4/Net-Ev-2.

### [172] [$μ$VLA: On Recurrent Memory for Partially Observable Manipulation in VLA Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12497)
*Egor Cherepanov,Nikita Kachaev,Daniil Zelezetsky,Aydar Bulatov,Artem Pshenitsyn,Yuri Kuratov,Alexey Skrynnik,Aleksandr I. Panov,Alexey K. Kovalev*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过在VLA模型中引入纯粹的自注意力记忆令牌机制，证明了极简的循环结构足以解决部分可观测性带来的决策难题，并为VLA模型中的记忆建模提供了一个高性能且易于分析的基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的记忆增强型视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型通常混合使用了循环、检索、压缩和辅助任务等多种复杂技术，导致难以分辨循环机制本身的真实贡献。本研究旨在通过受控隔离实验，评估简单递归架构在VLA模型中处理部分可观测性任务的有效性。

Method: 提出了一种名为μVLA的模型，在预训练的VLA主干网络中通过引入少量可学习的记忆令牌（memory tokens）来实现循环。该方法通过跨时间步的自注意力机制更新记忆，采用端到端的时间截断反向传播（TBPTT）进行训练，未引入任何辅助损失函数或复杂的架构变更，从而实现了对循环机制影响的纯粹隔离研究。

Result: 在MIKASA-Robo基准测试中，μVLA将五项训练任务的平均成功率从0.42大幅提升至0.84，并在保持零样本泛化能力方面优于无记忆基线（0.23对0.07）；在LIBERO数据集上达到96.2%的平均成功率，证明了在完全可观测场景下该方法不会造成性能回归。

Conclusion: 本研究通过受控实验确定了最小化骨干循环机制的能力边界。结果表明，仅通过在Transformer中引入学习型记忆令牌并进行时间截断反向传播（TBPTT），即可有效解决部分可观测性问题，且在完全可观测任务中不会导致性能下降。该研究为理解循环架构在VLA中的必要性提供了清晰的基准。

Abstract: Vision-language-action (VLA) models predict chunks of future actions from the current observation, an assumption that fails under partial observability, where decisions depend on information no longer visible. Existing memory-augmented VLAs simultaneously introduce recurrence, retrieval, compression modules, auxiliary objectives, hierarchical memory, or task-specific architectural changes, so the contribution of recurrence itself remains entangled with surrounding machinery. We present a controlled isolation study of recurrence in a strong pretrained VLA backbone. Our formulation augments the transformer with a small set of learnable memory tokens carried across timesteps and updated through self-attention, trained end to end with truncated backpropagation through time, with no auxiliary losses and no architectural changes. We instantiate this as $μ$VLA, a family of OpenVLA-OFT variants parameterized by memory width m, TBPTT length K, and the memory update rule (cross-step gradients or a detached EMA), so that recurrence is the only varying factor. On MIKASA-Robo, $μ$VLA improves average success rate on five training tasks from 0.42 to 0.84 at the strongest setting and reaches 0.23 on held-out tasks with the same memory structure versus 0.07 for the memoryless baseline. On tasks requiring different memory structure, performance remains near baseline. On LIBERO, the strongest recurrent variant achieves 96.2% average success, indicating no regression under full observability. We interpret these results as a calibration of the capability envelope of minimal in-backbone recurrence, identifying the regime in which it is sufficient and the regime where additional memory structure is required. Demos and videos can be found in https://avanturist322.github.io/mu-vla/.

</details>


### [173] [Improving Crash Frequency Prediction from Simulated Traffic Conflicts Using Machine Learning Based Microsimulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12500)
*Xian Liu,Carlo G. Prato,Gustav Markkula*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究验证了机器学习驱动的交通仿真模型在预测交通安全方面的有效性，发现相比传统模型，机器学习模型在无需额外校准的情况下能更准确地基于冲突预测事故，但指出其在模拟“事故发生”这一极端事件上仍需进一步改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的交通微观仿真模型多基于简化的规则模型，虽能模拟交通流，但在重现真实交通冲突动态方面存在缺陷，导致事故预测精度不足。研究旨在探讨机器学习模型通过学习大规模轨迹数据，是否能提升仿真的现实感及事故预测的准确性。

Method: 研究人员选取了英国利兹的五个真实信号交叉口作为样本，对比了传统规则驱动模型（rule-based model）与最先进的机器学习（ML）驾驶行为模型。通过二维碰撞时间（Time-to-Collision）指标识别模拟交通冲突，并利用极值理论（Extreme Value Theory）对事故频率进行预测，最后将结果与真实事故数据进行对比验证。

Result: 机器学习模型生成的冲突数据在事故预测方面与真实事故数据更为吻合，表现优于未经特定位置校准的规则模型。但研究同时发现，直接使用机器学习模型生成的“模拟事故”来预测现实事故频率的效果较差，说明机器学习模型目前能较好地重现日常冲突，但在模拟真实事故发生过程上仍有局限。

Conclusion: 基于机器学习的驾驶行为模型在模拟交通冲突以预测事故频率方面表现出巨大潜力，且无需进行繁琐的特定位置模型校准。然而，目前的机器学习模型尚无法直接生成真实的事故场景，未来研究需侧重于提升模型对极端冲突及事故诱发行为的模拟能力。

Abstract: Traffic microsimulation combined with surrogate safety measures has increasingly been used as a proactive alternative to historical crash data for predicting crash frequency for current or planned road infrastructure designs. However, existing microsimulation-based safety studies have adopted simplified rule-based behaviour models, which reproduce traffic flow reasonably well but often fail to generate realistic conflict dynamics, limiting crash prediction accuracy. Recent advances in machine learning (ML)-based behaviour models offer a promising opportunity to potentially improve microsimulation realism and crash frequency predictions by learning human driving behaviour directly from large-scale trajectory datasets. To investigate this possibility, traffic microsimulation was conducted for five real-world signalised intersections in Leeds, UK, using both a standard rule-based model and a state-of-the-art ML model. Simulated vehicle trajectories were analysed using a two-dimensional Time-to-Collision metric to identify simulated conflicts, which were then modelled using Extreme Value Theory to predict crash frequency. Results show that conflicts from the ML model yielded crash predictions in line with the real-world crash data, whereas the rule-based model did not permit meaningful predictions, presumably due to a lack of model calibration to the specific simulated intersections. Directly using ML-generated simulated crashes to predict real-world crash frequency also yielded poor results, suggesting that while current ML models can realistically reproduce conflicts, they are not yet able to generate realistic crashes. Overall, the findings demonstrate that ML-based behaviour models are promising for improving crash prediction from simulated conflicts, without a need for location-specific model calibration, and suggest clear future directions for ML-based traffic microsimulation.

### [176] [Boosting Direct Preference Optimization with Penalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12505)
*Pengwei Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DPOP是一种改进的离线偏好优化算法，它通过引入针对参考模型响应的门控惩罚机制，更有效地利用了模型自身的信息，在保持计算简便性的同时，显著提升了大型语言模型的对齐效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的离线偏好优化方法（如DPO）仅利用数据集中的成对响应，未能充分利用参考模型自身在给定提示下可能生成的响应信息，导致部分监督信号被浪费。

Method: 提出了一种名为DPOP的方法。该方法在DPO的损失函数中引入了一个“门控惩罚项”。当策略模型对偏好响应的分配概率仍低于拒绝响应时，该惩罚项会被激活，抑制模型生成与参考模型贪婪输出一致的次优回复，从而更有效地利用静态数据集之外的信息。

Result: 在AlpacaEval 2.0基准测试中，DPOP在Llama-3-8b-it和Gemma-2-9b-it模型上均优于DPO、SimPO和AlphaDPO，长度控制后的胜率分别相对提升了5.3%和4.4%。消融实验表明，SimNPO风格的长度归一化惩罚在当前设置下优于NPO和词元级别的可能性惩罚。

Conclusion: DPOP通过引入针对参考模型生成结果的门控惩罚机制，有效提升了离线偏好优化的性能。该方法在不增加额外训练开销的情况下，比DPO及其主流变体表现出更强的鲁棒性和竞争力。

Abstract: Offline preference optimization has become a practical substitute for reinforcement learning from human feedback, but pairwise objectives such as Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) and its variants use only the chosen and rejected responses stored in a static dataset. This leaves a useful signal unused: the response that the reference model itself would generate for the same prompt. We propose Direct Preference Optimization with Penalization (DPOP), a simple extension of DPO that augments the base preference loss with a gated penalty on reference-greedy responses. DPOP activates this penalty only when the current policy still assigns a lower likelihood to the preferred response than to the rejected response. On AlpacaEval 2.0, DPOP improves length-controlled win rate over DPO, SimPO, and AlphaDPO on both Llama-3-8b-it and Gemma-2-9b-it, achieving relative gains of 5.3\% and 4.4\% over baselines on the two models, respectively. Ablations further show that a SimNPO-style length-normalized penalty is stronger than NPO and token-level unlikelihood in this setting.

### [177] [Rubric-Guided Self-Distillation: Post-Training Without Rubric Verifiers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12507)
*MohammadHossein Rezaei,Anas Mahmoud,Zihao Wang,Utkarsh Tyagi,Advait Gosai,Razvan-Gabriel Dumitru,Aakash Sabharwal,Bing Liu,Yunzhong He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RGSD 提出了一种无需 LLM 判别器的自蒸馏训练框架，通过让模型学习如何根据评分标准生成内容，实现了比传统奖励机制更高效、更密集的策略优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于评分标准的训练方法严重依赖 LLM 判别器，这带来了高昂的训练开销，容易受到判别器固有偏见的影响，且将评分反馈压缩为稀疏的轨迹级信号，导致训练效率低下。因此，研究人员旨在寻找一种无需训练时判别器调用、反馈信号更密集且更高效的训练范式。

Method: 提出了“基于评分标准引导的自蒸馏”（Rubric-Guided Self-Distillation, RGSD）方法。该方法不再使用外部 LLM 判别器进行评分，而是训练一个能够根据给定评分标准（Rubric）生成输出的“教师策略模型”。随后，通过逐 token 的自蒸馏过程，将该教师模型的分布知识传递给“学生模型”（即无条件的模型），从而将稀疏的轨迹级奖励转化为密集的逐 token 学习信号。

Result: 在 Qwen-2.5 和 Qwen3-Thinking 模型系列上的实验表明，RGSD 在医学和科学领域的评分标准满足度上，可以达到与基于判别器的 GRPO 相当的水平，且显著降低了训练复杂度和开销。消融实验进一步证实，原始评分标准提供的引导信号优于自生成的参考回复。

Conclusion: RGSD 是一种高效、无需判别器的模型训练方法，通过将带评分标准的策略作为教师模型，将知识蒸馏到普通模型中，有效解决了传统基于判别器方法（如 GRPO）在推理成本、判别器偏见及奖励信号稀疏方面的缺陷。在资源受限或判别器不可靠的场景下，RGSD 是一个极具竞争力的替代方案。

Abstract: Rubrics have emerged as an alternative to RLVR in open-ended domains where a single ground-truth final answer is not available. Existing rubric-based training methods rely on an LLM verifier that scores each rollout against rubrics. This introduces substantial training-time overhead, exposes optimization to verifier-specific biases, and reduces rubric feedback to a sparse end-of-trajectory signal. We propose Rubric-Guided Self-Distillation (RGSD), a verifier-free training method in which the base policy, conditioned on the rubric, serves as the teacher for the unconditioned student. RGSD distills the rubric-conditioned teacher distribution into the student token-by-token, replacing sparse trajectory-level rewards with dense per-token learning signals and removing the LLM judge from the training loop entirely. Across Qwen-2.5 (3B, 7B) and Qwen3-Thinking (4B, 8B) models on medical and science domains, RGSD achieves rubric satisfaction comparable to judge-based GRPO while using one on-policy rollout per prompt and no training-time verifier calls. Ablations show that raw rubrics provide a stronger teacher enrichment signal than self-generated reference responses, while a stronger GRPO judge can outperform RGSD in some settings, positioning RGSD as a complementary verifier-free alternative when verifier cost or reliability is the bottleneck.

### [178] [Crossing the Validation Crisis: Cross-Validation Reduces Benchmarking Variance Surprisingly Well](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12552)
*Célestin Eve,Gaël Varoquaux,Thomas Moreau*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过引入“样本增益”概念并优化交叉验证流程，证明了增加交叉验证折数可显著提高机器学习模型评估的可靠性，并提出了动态停止策略以控制计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入“样本增益（sample gain）”概念，用于量化交叉验证通过多次拆分带来的数据扩增效果；提出一种动态提前停止交叉验证的程序，通过前几折的评估结果预测后续折数带来的收益，从而优化计算资源。

Result: 在合成数据集和真实数据集（组织病理学扫描及NLP微调）上的实验证明，多次拆分交叉验证能显著降低评估方差，提高估计的稳定性，且样本增益的边际效用递减出现得比预期更晚。

Conclusion: 通过增加交叉验证的折数，可以显著提升模型评估的稳健性与可靠性。研究提出的动态提前停止策略在保证评估精度的同时，有效平衡了计算成本。该方法为解决机器学习中的“验证危机”提供了一种有效且实用的路径。

Abstract: Modern machine learning progresses through empirical work, benchmarking new methods to evaluate relative performance. However, the statistical variability inherent to evaluation - exacerbated by the stochastic nature of many algorithms - often makes performance estimation unreliable due to the limited test samples available, leading to a validation crisis in which genuine advances are difficult to discern. In this work, we show that cross-validation improves markedly confidence when evaluating and comparing learning algorithm performances. We introduce the concept of sample gain, which quantifies the virtual data augmentation achieved by using multiple cross-validation splits to reduce benchmarking variance. Experiments on both synthetic and real-world datasets (histopathologic scans and NLP fine-tuning) demonstrate that multiple splits can substantially improve the reliability and stability of performance estimates, with diminishing returns often setting in later than expected. We also introduce a procedure to dynamically early-stop cross-validation by estimating from the first few folds if subsequent folds will bring large sample gains. Our findings highlight the value of pushing cross-validation on available samples to achieve robust and reliable benchmarking.

*Philipe Dias,Waqwoya Abebe,Abhishek Potnis,Aristeidis Tsaris,Dan Lu,Xiao Wang,Dalton Lunga*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究通过标准化实验条件实现“苹果对苹果”的公正对比：采用统一的自监督学习目标和相同的大规模预训练数据集，在控制模型参数量一致的前提下，于GEOBench基准测试集上对编码器-仅（encoder-only）、编码器-解码器（encoder-decoder）及掩码自动编码（masked autoencoding）等主流基础模型架构进行分类与分割任务评估。

Result: 研究量化了不同模型架构在处理多光谱数据时的表现差异，发现架构的灵活性（如对不同光谱波段的适应性）与下游任务性能之间存在显著的权衡关系，并明确了各类主流架构在地理空间多模态任务中的具体优势与局限性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过受控的基准测试，揭示了模型架构设计、模态对齐与下游任务表现之间的权衡关系。研究强调了在设计下一代地理空间基础模型时，应根据特定的灵活性需求和模态配置选择合适的架构，而非单纯追求某种特定的模型范式。

Abstract: Foundation models are rapidly transforming Earth observation by enabling scalable pretraining across diverse unlabeled geospatial modalities. However, their architectural diversity ranging from encoder-only to encoder-decoder and masked autoencoding paradigms makes it challenging to assess performance trade offs in a consistent manner. In this work, we present an apples-to-apples comparison of leading FM architectures designed for geospatial multimodal reasoning, with a particular focus on flexibility across varied spectral band configurations. We standardize pretraining using identical self supervised learning objectives and training datasets, and evaluate all models under consistent parameterization on the GEOBench benchmark across classification and segmentation tasks. Our results offer new insights into the design trade-offs between model flexibility, modality alignment, and downstream task performance. By highlighting architectural strengths and limitations under controlled conditions, this study provides practical guidance for building next generation geospatial foundation models capable of robust multimodal reasoning.

</details>


### [180] [Viral Proteins Reveal Geometry of Protein Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12609)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现嵌入空间存在一条“天然性”轴线，按困惑度将序列从细胞蛋白依次排列至随机序列；虽然模型规模的扩大不均匀地压缩了该轴线，但病毒蛋白在嵌入空间中仍保持了良好的线性可分性，表明模型能够超越浅层的困惑度指标，捕捉到深层的生物学特征。

Conclusion: 蛋白质语言模型（pLM）在嵌入空间中形成了一个以“天然性（nativeness）”为核心的全局结构，该结构虽受序列分布偏见影响，但并未掩盖模型对特定生物类别（如病毒）特有信息的捕捉能力，证实了pLM具备在高层语义表示中保留生物学特征的有效性。

Abstract: Protein language models are trained on highly imbalanced datasets, raising the question of how they represent underrepresented biological sequences. Using viral proteins as a case study across ESM model families, we identify a dominant nativeness axis in embedding space, aligned with masked reconstruction perplexity, that orders sequences from well-modeled cellular proteins through viral proteins to shuffled and random sequences. Scaling contracts this axis unevenly across viral families. Despite this, protein language model embeddings retain viral-specific signal: viral proteins remain linearly separable beyond zero-shot perplexity and shallow sequence features. Together, these results suggest that pLM representations are structured by a general notion of nativeness while preserving information specific to distinct biological groups.

### [181] [The Mathematics of AI Winters: The mathematical Taxonomy of Paradigm Fragility in AI Winter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12610)
*Miquel Noguer i Alonso,David Pacheco Aznar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出“AI寒冬”不只是炒作泡沫的破裂，更是早期AI研究在数学与计算复杂性方面触及客观科学瓶颈的结果，并分析了这些壁垒是如何被现代技术演进所逐步缓解的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有观点通常将“AI寒冬”归因于工程失败、商业失望或预期过高。本文旨在提供一个补充视角，论证当时的主流研究范式在客观上触及了表示能力、优化复杂性、统计学习能力及高维逼近等方面的数学形式化壁垒，从而解释了研究停滞的必然性。

Method: 作者采用综述与综合分析的方法，将历史上的AI研究低谷与当时计算机科学及统计学中的关键理论瓶颈（如感知机局限性、训练硬度、维数灾难、梯度消失等）进行对照分析，阐述了数学约束与研究范式转变之间的内在关联。

Result: 文章成功证明了早期AI研究面临的诸多挫折与特定的数学瓶颈（如Minsky和Papert的感知机不可行性、Blum和Rivest的训练复杂性、Stone的非参数估计极小极大速率，以及梯度消失问题）高度一致。这些障碍解释了AI发展的阶段性停滞，并揭示了随后的技术进步是如何在实际应用中缓解这些理论限制的。

Conclusion: 本文认为人工智能发展的低谷期不仅源于社会和商业因素，更深层次地受到数学与计算理论硬约束的限制。这些瓶颈并非被彻底消除，而是通过后续的技术突破（如深度学习、算力提升、算法优化等）被缓解或绕过，为理解AI发展的周期性提供了科学视角。

Abstract: Two major periods of reduced funding and confidence in artificial intelligence research, commonly called the first and second AI winters, are usually explained through engineering failure, commercial disappointment, and inflated expectations. This article develops a complementary thesis: that the dominant paradigms of those periods also met genuine formal barriers, including limitations of representation, optimisation, computational complexity, statistical learnability, and high-dimensional approximation. The contribution is synthetic rather than archival. We do not claim that particular theorems mechanically caused the winters; rather, we show that several central disappointments of early AI were aligned with mathematically precise bottlenecks. We analyse these bottlenecks through the perceptron impossibility results of Minsky and Papert, the complexity-theoretic hardness of exact neural-network training established by Blum and Rivest, minimax rates for nonparametric estimation in high dimension due to Stone, vanishing-gradient analyses by Hochreiter and by Bengio and collaborators, and classical statistical learning theory in the tradition of Vapnik and Chervonenkis, Valiant, and Blumer and collaborators. We then relate these barriers to the later breakthroughs that mitigated, rather than eliminated, them.

### [182] [Evaluation of AutoML Frameworks for IDS under Imbalanced Data Conditions of the NSL-KDD Dataset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12611)
*Wiliane Carolina Silva,Evandro César Vilas Boas,Felipe A. P. de Figueiredo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过分析九种AutoML框架在严重不平衡的NSL-KDD数据集上的表现，揭示了单纯的准确率优化无法有效检测稀有攻击，并指出原生集成不平衡处理机制对提升多分类入侵检测性能至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的入侵检测研究常通过简化为二分类或删除少数类来处理数据集不平衡问题，缺乏对真实场景下严重多分类不平衡问题的深入研究。该论文旨在评估AutoML框架在保持原始数据分布情况下的实际表现，以弥补当前研究中对不平衡感知学习行为评估的缺失。

Method: 该研究采用九种开源AutoML框架，在保持NSL-KDD数据集原始五分类分布（包含严重不平衡的R2L和U2R攻击）的前提下，构建了统一且可复现的实验协议。通过比较不同框架在架构设计、集成策略、超参数优化和不平衡处理机制上的差异，深入分析了它们对少数类别的识别能力。

Result: 实验表明，集成学习和不平衡感知优化策略能显著提升少数类别的识别效果。PyCaret表现最佳（宏F1分数为66%），其次是AutoGluon（55%）。研究证实，仅依赖准确率导向的优化方法在面对高不平衡的入侵检测场景时，会导致在稀有攻击类别上的泛化能力较差。

Conclusion: 该研究为基于AutoML的入侵检测系统在严重多分类不平衡场景下建立了标准化的评估基准，指出目前大多数AutoML框架在处理稀有攻击类型时存在局限，强调了将不平衡感知优化、重采样技术及分层评估策略原生集成到自动化机器学习流水线中的必要性。

Abstract: This work investigates the impact of severe class imbalance on the performance of automated machine learning (AutoML) frameworks for multiclass network intrusion detection using the NSL-KDD dataset. Unlike previous studies that simplify the problem through binary classification or minority-class removal, we preserve the original five-class distribution, including highly underrepresented attacks such as R2L and U2R, enabling a realistic evaluation of imbalance-sensitive learning behavior. Nine open-source AutoML frameworks were analyzed under a unified and reproducible experimental protocol, considering differences in architectural design, ensemble strategies, validation procedures, hyperparameter optimization, and imbalance-handling mechanisms. The results demonstrate that frameworks incorporating ensemble learning and imbalance-aware optimization achieve better minority-class discrimination. PyCaret obtained the best overall performance, reaching 66\% macro-F1, followed by AutoGluon with 55\%, whereas frameworks lacking native balancing support exhibited significant degradation in minority-class detection capability. The analysis further shows that accuracy-oriented optimization alone is insufficient for highly imbalanced IDS scenarios, since high-weighted metrics may coexist with poor generalization on rare attack categories. As a contribution, this work establishes a standardized benchmark for AutoML-based intrusion detection under severe multiclass imbalance, highlighting current architectural limitations and the need for native integration of imbalance-aware optimization, resampling, and stratified evaluation strategies into automated learning pipelines. The source code is publicly available.

### [183] [Towards Provably Fair Machine Learning: Bayesian Approaches For Consistent and Transparent Predictions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12615)
*Owen O'Neill,Fintan Costello*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对机器学习模型在细粒度子组上预测不一致的问题，提出了一种“公平贝叶斯分类器”。该分类器通过强制执行确定性和统计一致性，并引入拒绝预测机制，在确保各子组预测质量的同时，有效提升了模型在少数群体中的公平性与准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器学习的高风险应用中，模型表现往往在不同子组间存在系统性差异，且现有的正则化方法在提升整体性能时，会以牺牲少数群体子组的准确性为代价。现有模型在细粒度子组上的预测往往与观察到的数据不一致，缺乏有效的公平性保障。

Method: 作者提出了“公平贝叶斯分类器”（Fair Bayesian classifier）。该方法基于“确定性”（完全相同的个体获得相同的预测）和“统计一致性”（预测结果与该子组的贝叶斯最优目标分布在统计上无显著差异）两个核心要求。模型在无法做出一致且确定性的预测时会选择拒绝预测，从而在所有子组中同时强制执行上述要求。

Result: 在Adult、COMPAS和Bank Marketing数据集上的实验表明，标准分类器在大量子组上存在统计不一致性。新提出的分类器通过结构设计实现了零一致性误差，且在准确率和多校准（multicalibration）指标上均优于基线模型。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过在数据所支持的最细粒度上强制执行贝叶斯一致性，并结合有原则的拒绝预测机制，可以实现实质性的子组公平性。统计一致性为模型性能评估提供了坚实的理论基础，是解决算法公平性问题、特别是针对弱势群体子组推理问题的关键路径。

Abstract: ML classifiers deployed in high-stakes domains produce predictions whose quality varies systematically across subgroups. For granular subgroups defined by intersections of multiple features, predictions are often inconsistent with the observed data: the model's outputs contradict the evidence available for that subgroup. This problem is exacerbated by regularisation, which improves aggregate performance by collapsing small subgroups into larger groups, disproportionately affecting demographic minorities. We define two requirements for consistent prediction: determinism (identical individuals receive identical predictions) and statistical consistency (we cannot reject, at significance level alpha, the hypothesis that the predictions for a subgroup were drawn from the Bayesian optimal target distribution inferred for that subgroup). From these requirements we derive the Fair Bayesian classifier, which enforces both across every group and subgroup simultaneously and abstains whenever no consistent deterministic prediction is possible. On three benchmark datasets (Adult, COMPAS, and Bank Marketing), standard classifiers produce statistically inconsistent predictions for a substantial proportion of subgroups. Our classifier achieves zero consistency error by construction while exceeding baseline accuracy and multicalibration on every dataset tested. Statistical consistency provides a principled foundation for prediction quality with direct implications for algorithmic fairness. Minority demographics are disproportionately concentrated in small subgroups, precisely where frequentist inference is least reliable; addressing this inference problem is therefore a necessary step toward fair ML. By enforcing Bayesian consistency at the finest resolution the data supports, the our classifier demonstrates that exhaustive subgroup fairness with principled abstention is achievable in practice.

</details>


### [184] [Bag of Dims: Training-Free Mechanistic Interpretability via Dimension-Level Sign Patterns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12629)
*Varun Reddy Nalagatla*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究发现Transformer的原始隐藏状态维度天生就具备语义解耦特性，通过“Bag of Dims”方法，仅需极少量计算即可在无需任何训练的情况下，直接从标准基中提取大量高可解释性的语义特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决现有深度学习可解释性研究中通常需要昂贵的训练、优化或复杂的字典学习（如稀疏自编码器）来解耦潜在特征的问题，探索Transformer标准基（Standard Basis）本身是否就蕴含了可读的语义特征。

Method: 提出了“Bag of Dims”框架，利用Transformer隐藏状态的维度符号（正负）表示语义内容，数值大小表示置信度。通过单向传递（单次前向传播）计算词表标记的维度符号一致性，无需训练，利用汉明距离（Hamming scoring）及轴对齐加权进行特征提取与验证。

Result: 在Qwen、Gemma、Mistral等模型上验证了该方法：仅使用符号模式即可实现72-93%的Top-5预测准确率；无训练发现175个语义类别（平均AUC 0.80）；证实了特征在维度间高度解耦（互信息仅0.0014 bits），且FFN神经元与这些特征存在强对应关系。

Conclusion: 本研究提出Transformer的标准基本身就构成了高效的语义特征空间。通过“Bag of Dims”框架，证明了无需训练即可直接提取高质量语义特征，这不仅简化了可解释性研究的流程，也挑战了“必须通过复杂变换才能提取解耦特征”的传统观点。

Abstract: We show that the standard basis of transformer hidden states already provides a training-free, architecture-general feature basis. Individual dimensions encode semantic content via their signs and confidence via their magnitudes, functioning as independent binary registers. We validate this Bag of Dims framework across three model families (Qwen 3.5-4B, Gemma 3-4B, Mistral 7B) through four progressive experiments. Sign patterns alone carry predictive content: replacing all magnitudes with unity achieves 72-93% top-5 next-token accuracy through the LM head, and pure Hamming scoring without any decoder reaches 80-90% top-4096. These sign patterns organize into semantic features: using a single-token type cache (one forward pass per vocabulary token, no context), we discover 175 categories via per-dimension sign consistency (mean AUC 0.80) from 50 anchors with zero training. A trained probe adds only +0.018 AUC and converges to axis-aligned weights, confirming negligible cross-dimension structure. This structure extends to attention: all 175 categories remain discoverable in K and V projections. On the write side, static FFN weight inspection links 20% of features to individual writer neurons (>0.70 agreement; random controls: 0%), with top-200 neuron coalitions achieving >0.70 agreement on 99.9% of prototypes via majority vote. Fully unsupervised discovery (random seeds, no labels) scales to 1500 features at 100% yield and 99% sparsity across all three models, with pairwise MI of 0.0014 bits confirming low inter-dimension coupling. These results establish that the standard basis already suffices for feature reading throughout the transformer compute pathway, requiring no training, no optimization, and no GPU-days beyond a single forward pass per vocabulary token.

</details>


### [185] [Keep Policy Gradient in Charge: Sibling-Guided Credit Distillation for Long-Horizon Tool-Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12634)
*Tianyu Ding,Jianhong Xin,Juan Pablo De la Cruz Weinstein*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对长程工具使用任务中奖励稀疏和自蒸馏易引入错误偏差的问题，本文提出了SGCD方法，通过对比同伴轨迹并重塑token信用分配，在不增加推理成本的前提下显著提升了模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在长程工具使用任务中，强化学习的奖励往往只能在轨迹末端获得，导致难以直接为中间的推理、API调用及回答token分配信用。现有的自蒸馏方法虽然旨在增强信号，但往往会因无法区分奖励来源而同时放大有用技能与有害捷径，导致模型性能受损。

Method: 本文提出了“同伴引导的信用蒸馏”（Sibling-Guided Credit Distillation, SGCD）。该方法通过对比成功与失败的同伴轨迹（sibling rollouts），利用外部LLM生成逐步信用参考，并结合师生分歧（teacher/student divergence）来重塑GRPO的token级优势。在训练中，模型学习的是信用分配而非直接模仿动作，且推理阶段无需额外辅助。

Result: 在AppWorld和$\tau^3$-airline基准测试中，SGCD的表现均优于标准的GRPO算法。具体而言，在AppWorld的test_normal集上TGC从42.9提升至45.6，test_challenge集从24.7提升至27.0；在$\tau^3$-airline上，pass@1准确率从0.583提升至0.602。

Conclusion: 研究表明，直接的token级自蒸馏在长程工具使用任务中可能因盲目模仿而导致模型表现下降。SGCD通过将蒸馏聚焦于信用分配而非单纯的动作模仿，有效解决了这一问题，为提升复杂推理任务中的强化学习效率提供了一种新范式。

Abstract: Long-horizon tool-use reinforcement learning can learn from outcome verification, but its
  trajectory-level advantage is broadcast across many reasoning, API, and answer tokens.
  Self-distillation promises a denser signal by reusing a policy's own rollouts or a privileged
  teacher. We show, however, that direct token-level self-distillation can silently destroy tool use:
  it rehearses teacher behavior without knowing which actions the verifier rewards, so useful skills
  and harmful shortcuts are amplified together. We introduce Sibling-Guided Credit Distillation
  (SGCD), which uses distillation for credit assignment rather than as a competing actor loss.
  Dynamic sampling produces mixed successful and failed sibling rollouts; an external LLM summarizes
  their contrast into a training-only stepwise credit reference; dense teacher/student divergence
  drives credit reassignment; and bounded detached credit weights reshape GRPO token advantages. The
  deployed student sees no external LLM, sibling evidence, or oracle. Across AppWorld and
  $τ^3$-airline, SGCD improves over matched GRPO comparators: AppWorld TGC $42.9 \to 45.6$ on
  test_normal and $24.7 \to 27.0$ on test_challenge, and $τ^3$-airline pass@1 $0.583 \to 0.602$.

</details>


### [186] [The Metric Picks the Winner: Evaluation Choice Flips Model Rankings for Drug-Response Prediction in Unseen Chemistry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12639)
*Dhruv Agarwal,Riya Bisht*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究针对“未见药物转录组响应预测”这一难题，证明了评估指标的选择直接决定了模型表现的优劣，并提出了一种融合化学嵌入与检索特征的深度学习框架，该框架在特定评价指标下显著超越了简单基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在计算细胞生物学中，预测细胞对“未见”药物的转录组响应是一项核心挑战。现有的复杂模型在处理新化学结构的化合物时，往往难以超越简单的基准模型。本研究旨在探讨如何通过合理的指标设定和模型架构来提升此类预测的准确性。

Method: 提出了一种分阶段的建模方法：首先使用“简单基线”（未处理对照和训练化合物均值），接着使用基于非参数检索的策略（基于Tanimoto相似度加权），最后通过融合化学嵌入与检索特征的深度学习模型进行残差预测，并引入不确定性估计和基因程序分析。

Result: 实验发现，当使用不同的评估指标时，模型排名会发生逆转。在特定的加权指标（wMSE）下，深度融合模型显著优于线性指纹基准模型；而在其他代理指标下，简单的线性回归反而表现最好。这一发现证明了指标校准在药物响应预测任务中的关键作用。

Conclusion: 研究强调了评估指标对于衡量模型在“未见药物”预测任务中性能的决定性影响。在评估机制不匹配的情况下，模型优劣的排序可能完全颠倒。因此，在药物基因组学研究中，确保指标与生物学任务的实际目标高度一致至关重要。

Abstract: Predicting how a cell's transcriptome responds to a drug it has never seen is a core, hard problem in computational cell biology: recent benchmarks show complex models often fail to beat trivial baselines once test compounds are held out by chemistry. We study one cell line and assay, THP-1 cells profiled by DRUG-seq, scored by the active-compound weighted MSE(wMSE) of the VCPI prediction contest. We propose a staged approach: dumb baselines (untreated control and mean training-compound response) that the field keeps failing to beat; non-parametric retrieval (a Tanimoto-weighted average of a held-out compound's nearest training compounds); and a fusion stage combining a frozen chemistry embedding with retrieval-support features to predict the residual over the mean, with an uncertainty head and gene programs. On the released VCPI THP-1 drug-seq data (14,026 training compounds), under a Bemis-Murcko scaffold split, the model ranking inverts depending on the metric. Under an inverse-variance per-gene proxy, a regularized linear regression on Morgan fingerprints appears to win over the deep models, retrieval, and ChemBERTa -- the textbook "simple baselines win" result. But under the contest's true active-set metric (per-(gene, compound) Mejia weights, validated against the official scorer; mean baseline 0.535 vs the organizers' 0.507 reference), that reverses: the deep models win, our fusion decoder significantly beats the linear fingerprint baseline (-0.012 wMSE, paired bootstrap p < 10^-4), and the proxy's winner becomes the worst chemistry-aware predictor. Picking the metric picks the winner -- to our knowledge the first demonstration on real held-out drug chemistry of the metric-calibration effect established largely on genetic perturbation. We release a reproducible pipeline
  wired to the official scorer that emits a valid submission over the real 1064 x 12,995 grid.

</details>

### [188] [TEDD: Robust Detection of Unstable Temporal Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12643)
*Ricardo Ribeiro Pereira,Bruno Casal Laraña,Nádia Soares,Miguel Araújo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对机器学习模型在时序数据中因分布偏移导致性能下降的问题，本文提出了一种名为TEDD的自动化方法。该方法通过将特征偏移检测转化为时间戳预测任务，能够高效、准确地识别导致模型不稳定的特征，且具有无需调参、可扩展性强等优点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界的时序数据往往存在分布偏移（Distribution Drift），直接使用此类数据训练机器学习模型会导致模型性能快速下降。现有手段缺乏自动识别哪些特征随时间变化并导致模型不稳定的能力，因此需要一种自动化方法来定位这些特征，以辅助数据科学家进行模型维护和优化。

Method: 作者提出了TEDD（Temporal Drift Detection）技术。该方法核心思想是将时间偏移检测建模为一个回归问题：利用回归模型根据特征值来预测实例的时间戳。如果模型能够很好地根据特定特征预测时间戳，则说明该特征分布随时间发生了变化。通过分析特征对预测任务的贡献度，即可定位导致模型不稳定的特定特征。

Result: 实验表明，TEDD能够成功检测所有类型的基本偏移模式（包括数值型和类别型特征），具备多变量偏移检测能力，能对特征偏移程度进行量化，且在无需参数调整的情况下，在特征数量和样本数量上均表现出良好的可扩展性，性能优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出的TEDD方法通过预测时间戳来检测特征偏移，不仅能够有效识别数值型和类别型特征的各类基本偏移模式，还具有多变量偏移检测能力、无需调参且具备良好的可扩展性，为构建更鲁棒的机器学习模型提供了有效的自动化辅助工具。

Abstract: When working with real-world temporal data, it is common to encounter features whose distribution is changing over time. The naive employment of Machine Learning models on this unstable data might lead to rapidly degrading performance, especially if the new distribution is much different from what was previously seen during training. In order to cope with this problem, it is critical to automatically identify features that are changing over time. With these features detected, data scientists and other practitioners will be able to mitigate the issue (for instance, by applying data transformations), deploying more robust models that retain high performance for longer periods of time. In this paper, we describe which temporal changes a feature should not suffer from, and propose TEDD, a technique to a) identify when a dataset might lead to an unstable Machine Learning model and b) automatically detect which features cause such lack of robustness. In order to achieve it, we leverage a regression model to highlight which features contribute to a good prediction of an instance's timestamp. We compare our approach to other methods in real and synthetic data, testing their detection capability on all simple change patterns. We show that our method: detects all types of basic changes, both for numerical and categorical features; can detect multivariate drifts; returns a comparable value measuring the amount of change of each feature; requires no parameter tuning; and is scalable both on number of features and instances of the dataset.

</details>


### [189] [Physics-Aware Auxiliary Losses Improve Out-of-Distribution Generalization of a GNN Synthesizability Filter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12651)
*Riya Bisht,Dhruv Agarwal*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的药物合成可行性评估工具（如SAScore等）主要依赖统计方法，在生成模型提出远离训练数据的分子（分布外，OOD）时，其性能会显著下降。因此，研究旨在探讨将廉价、闭式物理先验作为辅助监督引入图神经网络，是否能提升模型在OOD场景下的泛化性能。

Method: 该研究在GINE图神经网络主干网络的基础上，引入了两项物理辅助损失：一是基于Bertz指标的拓扑复杂度回归，二是基于MMFF94力场能量的应变能软惩罚。研究通过在HIV、Tox21和COCONUT数据集上构建OOD分割，并对比四种变体（基线、+复杂度、+应变能、+两者结合）的表现来验证模型性能。

Conclusion: 在分布外（OOD）评估中，引入物理先验（拓扑复杂度和应变能）作为图神经网络的辅助监督，能够显著提升分子合成可行性预测的泛化能力。此外，研究强调了在药物发现任务中进行多随机种子评估对于获得稳健结果的重要性。

Abstract: Machine-learning drug-discovery pipelines increasingly rely on generative models that propose molecules far from the data used to train downstream synthesizability filters. Existing filters (SAScore, SCScore, RAscore, DeepSA) are purely statistical and degrade in exactly this out-of-distribution (OOD) regime. We ask whether cheap, closed-form physical priors, used as auxiliary supervision on a graph neural network (GNN), improve OOD generalization. We add two auxiliary losses to a GINE backbone: a topological complexity regression supervised by the Bertz index, and a strain-energy soft penalty supervised by MMFF94 force-field energy. On a 65,177-molecule corpus (HIV, Tox21, COCONUT) labeled by SAScore thresholds we reproduce a strong in-distribution baseline, then evaluate a 4-way ablation (baseline / +complexity / +strain / +both) on a single-source OOD split (train on drug-like HIV+Tox21, test on COCONUT natural products), repeated over 5 seeds with paired bootstrap confidence intervals. All three physics-aware variants give a small but statistically significant OOD improvement over the baseline (mean OOD AUC 0.9774): +complexity Delta = +0.0060 (95% CI [+0.0023, +0.0102]), +strain Delta = +0.0032 ([+0.0008, +0.0052]), +both Delta = +0.0066 ([+0.0038, +0.0093]); every interval excludes zero, and the combination is best. The variants are indistinguishable in-distribution, so the effect is visible only under OOD evaluation. We are explicit that the effects are modest, and we report a cautionary methodological finding: a single-seed version of this experiment produced a qualitatively different (non-monotone) story that did not survive multi-seed evaluation.

*Riya Bisht,Dhruv Agarwal*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究人员将物理信息神经网络（PINN）应用于两室药物动力学模型，通过将微分方程作为惩罚项引入损失函数，并与非线性最小二乘法（NLS）和纯数据驱动的多层感知机（MLP）进行基准对比。研究测试了线性模型和具有饱和消除特征的Michaelis-Menten模型，并探讨了加入稀疏组织观测数据对模型可识别性的影响。

Result: 在简单的线性模型中，PINN达到了与NLS相当的精度，并能同时推导出组织浓度曲线；在更复杂的Michaelis-Menten模型中，PINN揭示了从血浆数据推导参数的不可识别性（传统方法则会产生误导性结果）；加入少量稀疏观测后，PINN能有效恢复模型关键参数。

Conclusion: PINN提供了一种通用的建模方法，在传统方法有效的情况下表现相当，在复杂或不可识别的情况下能揭示结构性问题，并能灵活整合稀疏数据，是药物动力学分析的有力补充。

Abstract: Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) are an attractive tool for partial-observation problems in biology, where the governing dynamics are known but some compartments cannot be measured. Chemotherapy pharmacokinetics (PK) is a clean instance: drug concentration in plasma is routinely measured, but concentration in tissue -- which determines tumour kill and off-target toxicity -- is not. We benchmark a PINN against the standard clinical baseline (nonlinear least-squares on the analytical biexponential plasma solution, hereafter NLS) and a physics-agnostic neural baseline (a data-only MLP) on two PK problems. On the linear two-compartment problem, NLS is near-optimal; the PINN matches it to within a small constant factor while also producing the tissue curve in a single training pass, whereas the data-only MLP fails on tissue by roughly 10x. On a Michaelis-Menten extension (saturable elimination), the biexponential closed form no longer exists, so NLS is mis-specified and silently returns meaningless rate constants. The PINN instead exposes a deeper fact: the Michaelis-Menten two-compartment model is non-identifiable from plasma alone, and the PINN reports this honestly by converging to a basin with k12 -> 0. Adding two sparse tissue observations largely resolves identifiability: across five seeds the PINN recovers k21 to within 1% of truth and Vmax, Km to within one standard-deviation bar, while k12 moves in the correct direction (0.02 -> 0.82) but remains ~2 sigma below truth -- a recovery the closed-form NLS estimator cannot attempt at all, because its biexponential ansatz describes only plasma. Our claim is not that PINNs beat NLS. It is that PINNs offer a uniform recipe that ties the textbook estimator on the textbook problem, exposes structural identifiability that
  the textbook estimator hides, and absorbs heterogeneous measurements within a single loss.

  <summary>Details</summary>

To address this challenge, we propose AlignGAD, a zero-shot generalized graph anomaly detection framework. Our framework is built upon three key components: a Global Unification Module that aligns heterogeneous node features and normalizes graph signals in the spectral domain; a Clustering Module that constructs cluster-aware graph views to capture group-level abnormal patterns; and a Node Discrepancy Scoring Module that measures reconstruction discrepancy and aggregates anomaly evidence from different graph views. Experiments on multiple real-world datasets demonstrate the effectiveness of AlignGAD under the zero-shot GAD setting.

### [192] [Fed-FBD: Federated Functional Block Diversification for Isolation, Privacy, and Surgical Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12679)
*Weijie Chen,Alan B. McMillan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对联邦学习的安全与隐私缺陷，本文提出Fed-FBD架构，通过将模型拆解为可追踪的功能模块，实现了恶意攻击隔离、原生隐私保护及高效的机器遗忘，且精度损失极小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的联邦学习方法（如FedAvg）将参与者视为黑盒，无法有效隔离恶意贡献者、审计单个客户端的影响力，也难以在用户退出时实现符合“被遗忘权”的精确模型删除。

Method: 提出了一种名为“联邦功能块多样化”（Fed-FBD）的模块化架构。该方法将ResNet主干网络分解为6个功能块，并维护一个包含N个“颜色变体”（color variants）的仓库。每个变体由独立追踪且带有贡献者标记的模块组装而成，从而实现细粒度的贡献审计和隔离。

Result: 在MedMNIST和CIFAR-10数据集上的实验表明，Fed-FBD在IID数据集上仅损失0.3%-3.1%的精度；在非IID环境下（Dirichlet alpha=1.0）表现稳健；同时能够成功限制恶意攻击的影响，并实现毫秒级的“手术式”模型遗忘。

Conclusion: Fed-FBD 通过模块化架构有效地解决了联邦学习中的模型污染、隐私泄露和删除遗忘权三大核心挑战，在牺牲极小精度损失的前提下，为联邦学习系统提供了更好的鲁棒性、安全性和可追溯性。

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) enables collaborative model training without sharing raw patient data, but standard approaches such as FedAvg treat each client as a black box and provide no mechanism for isolating an adversarial contributor, auditing per-client influence, or honoring a departed participant's right to be forgotten. We present Fed-FBD (Federated Functional Block Diversification), a modular federated architecture that decomposes a ResNet backbone into six functional blocks (the stem, four residual groups, and the classification head) and maintains a warehouse of N color variants, each assembled from independently tracked and contributor-stamped blocks. Fed-FBD provides three capabilities absent in FedAvg: (i) architecturally guaranteed block-level isolation, so that an adversarial or mislabelled client cannot contaminate the clean colous; (ii) privacy-by-design, where membership inference advantage is already indistinguishable from chance before any privacy mechanism is applied; and (iii) surgical machine unlearning of a departed participant's contribution at sub-second cost and without retraining. Experiments on six MedMNIST-2D datasets, PathMNIST at 224x224, and CIFAR-10 show that Fed-FBD trades a modest 0.3%-3.1% IID accuracy gap on the adequately sized datasets for these guarantees, remains within 0.8%-4.0% of FedAvg at Dirichlet alpha=1.0 on three of four datasets, and confines all six adversarial attacks we study to the poisoned client's own blocks with at most +/-0.01 AUC drift on the clean colors.

### [193] [How Useful is Causal Invariance for Domain Adaptation in Finite-Sample Settings?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12680)
*Julia Kostin,Kasra Jalaldoust,Elias Bareinboim,Samory Kpotufe,Fanny Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过线性回归模型分析了因果知识在监督领域自适应中的作用，提出了基于因果不变性构建候选预测器的框架，并证明了性能提升取决于目标风险边际的显著性，明确了因果知识能够提升模型性能的理论边界与限制条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决机器学习模型在分布偏移（Domain Shift）下性能退化的问题。尽管现有基于因果的方法能够发现跨域不变预测器，但其在有限样本监督领域自适应（sDA）场景下的具体增益及其边界条件尚不明确。该研究旨在证明在何种条件下，因果知识能确实为sDA带来有限样本上的性能提升。

Method: 以线性回归为研究框架，利用已知或部分已知的因果知识，定义出一系列具有不变性或潜在不变性的特征子集及对应的候选预测器；提出了一种自适应聚合算法（Adaptive Aggregation Procedure），并通过推导上界和下界来量化分析有限样本下的预测误差，将其与目标风险边际及结构性偏移大小联系起来。

Result: 推导出了衡量sDA性能提升的理论界，证明了当目标风险边际相对于目标样本量足够大时，算法能够选择最优候选器并避免负迁移；若边际过小，则无法通过因果知识获得超越仅使用目标数据的性能提升。实验在真实因果基准测试上验证了这些理论发现。

Conclusion: 研究表明，因果知识在监督领域自适应（sDA）中具有显著潜力，但其性能提升高度依赖于目标风险边际与有限样本估计误差之间的权衡。在因果知识充分且结构性偏移显著的情况下，通过自适应聚合算法可以有效实现性能优化；反之，若因果结构提供的区分度不足，则因果知识的引入无法提供实质性的有限样本速率优势。

Abstract: Machine learning models often degrade when they are deployed on a target distribution that differs from the source distributions they were trained on. Recent work in causality-based domain generalization has shown how shared causal structure between domains can induce invariant predictors, e.g., models on a subset of features which have stable risk across structured domain shifts. However, the extent to which such population-level causal invariances can lead to gains in finite-sample settings remains underexplored. In particular, in practice we often have access to a few labeled target samples, a setting called supervised domain adaptation (sDA). In this paper, we explore when (full or partial) causal knowledge can provably improve supervised domain adaptation.
  As a first step, we study linear regression, where full or partial causal knowledge specifies a collection of invariant or possibly invariant feature subsets, each yielding a source-trained candidate predictor. We derive matching upper and lower bounds showing that finite-sample gains are governed by the target-risk margins separating the candidates, together with the finite-source estimation error. When these margins are sufficiently large relative to $n_Q$, an adaptive aggregation procedure can match the best candidate predictor while avoiding negative transfer relative to target-only learning. On the other hand, when the margins are too small, no algorithm can reliably exploit the candidate collection to obtain faster finite-sample rates. We further connect these margins to structural shift magnitude in linear SCMs and validate the theory on real-world causal benchmarks.
